Current Affairs Commentary

Tragedy in Austria 64

— Hua

According to a telegram from Vienna, the Austrian capital, the day before yesterday, the Austrian cabinet held an emergency meeting. It has granted the greatest authority to Chancellor Schuschnigg, creating Schuschnigg's sole personal dictatorship. At the same time, the Homeland Security Force and other political and military organizations were dissolved. Prince Starhemberg, the leader of the Homeland Security Force, has fled abroad, ending his political life. This important change seems to have brought the internal disputes in Austria over the past few months or years to an end. In the future, there may be a more stable situation in this vital piece of land in Central Europe. However, if we examine Austria's internal and external affairs more deeply, we will feel that Austria, situated between two fascist ambitious nations, will inevitably be at the mercy of others and become a victim of aggression if it does not have an independent internal and external policy. In other words, its fate will forever be a tragedy.

Naturally, when we look back at history, we know that Austria since the Great War has had its territory greatly reduced and its economic destiny controlled by Britain and France, and has long been trapped in a tragic situation. However, we will see that Austria's greater tragedy began in 1934. Originally, Austria after the war was governed by the Social Democratic Party. Although the social policies implemented were not thorough, they were still much more progressive than the capitalist countries of Western Europe. In particular, the workers' dormitories in Vienna benefited 500,000 civilians and gained very good international reputation. However, this aroused the jealousy of Italy. In February 1934, Dollfuss, who called himself a "little Napoleon," used international fascism as his background to eliminate the Social Democratic Party and create a dictatorship. However, the expansion of Dollfuss' power aroused the concerns of the German National Socialist Party. In June of the same year, a National Socialist coup occurred in Vienna, and Dollfuss was also tragically killed. However, the intrusion of the National Socialist forces into Austria was not tolerated by Britain, France, and Italy. Therefore, although the National Socialists killed Dollfuss, the coup did not succeed. At this time, Britain and France supported Schuschnigg, whom they favored, to maintain the independent situation. Italy, on the other hand, used Prince Starhemberg as a tool to strengthen the power of his semi-fascist Homeland Security Force, seemingly becoming the protector of the semi-colonial Austria. This complicated situation, due to the serious threat of the National Socialist Party, caused the contradictions between France and Italy to transform into understanding, and surprisingly maintained for nearly two years. However, Austria's independence was only nominal. It was a well-known fact that its internal and external policies had to obey the actual rulers. The most obvious example is that when the League of Nations resolved to impose sanctions on Italy, Austria, intimidated by the power of its strong neighbor, did not dare to participate at all. The loss of diplomatic autonomy by a semi-colonial country can be seen from this.

On July 11 of this year, the German-Austrian Compromise Agreement was concluded, which was actually initiated by Italy. This negotiation was carried out as a result of Mussolini summoning Schuschnigg to the Rocca delle Camminate villa on June 5 to personally instruct him. As for the downfall of Prince Starhemberg, the tragic consequences of a semi-colonial country having no autonomy in its internal affairs are even more evident. Originally, Starhemberg's rise to power was due to Italy's desire to use him. However, recently Starhemberg suddenly had personal ambitions, hoping to become the regent after the restoration of the Austrian monarchy. This aroused Italy's disgust. Therefore, Schuschnigg seized the opportunity to exclude the disgraced Starhemberg. However, now, due to the result of the German-Austrian Compromise, the power of the National Socialist Party has gradually increased in the Austrian cabinet. Schuschnigg's own fate is as unreliable as Starhemberg's. The compromise between the two fascist ambitious nations, Italy and Germany, on the Austrian issue will eventually break down and return to the original sharp struggle.

In short, from the current changes in the Austrian political situation, what we see is always a tragedy caused by a semi-colonial country not struggling towards the road of independence and freedom. Our country is currently standing at such a crossroads. We should also take the lesson of Austria as a serious warning.

Administrative Reform Plan: The Japanese Political Situation Is Seriously Undercut; The Current Cabinet Tries Its Best to Compile the Budget; The Military and the Prime Minister Disagree 65

(Tokyo) The government and the military have conflicting opinions on the issue of reforming the administrative structure, which may lead to a political crisis. This is a major political issue. According to the opinions of Prime Minister Hirota and other cabinet members, the current cabinet should do its best to ensure the successful completion of next year's budget. However, dealing with the issue of reforming the administrative organs before the budget issue is resolved will hinder the compilation of next year's budget. Therefore, compiling the budget is the prior problem. The military's proposed plan to reform the administrative organs should only be considered after next year's budget. However, the military holds the opposite view, believing that the government's delay in reforming the issue violates the spirit of revitalizing the administration. The military's opinions are quite strong. It is noteworthy whether Prime Minister Hirota can reach a compromise when negotiating with them. (Kyodo News, December 12)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Terauchi recently submitted a plan to reform the administrative organs. The political circles are debating this fiercely, and it is feared that it will eventually lead to a serious political crisis. The plan has attracted the deep attention of the whole country. At the same time, some people have refuted it, saying that it cannot be implemented. However, the military is determined to achieve its goals. However, those in the cabinet who oppose the Army Minister's plan occupy considerable power. Although the Prime Minister has the sincerity to follow the military's proposal, he also firmly believes that this plan cannot be fully endorsed, and at least must be delayed for some time. The public wants to implement this reform, and the cabinet can only resign en masse. However, the Prime Minister believes that at this time of international tension, it is not appropriate to rashly change the cabinet. It is currently difficult to predict how this matter will develop. (Reuters, December 12)

(Tokyo) The army authorities' attitude on the issue of reforming the administrative structure is quite strong. After Army Minister Terauchi returned to Tokyo on the 12th, this issue must have a concrete development. The specific guidelines of the Army Ministry's proposal to establish a minister without portfolio are roughly as follows:

(1) The first method to control important national policy agencies is to merge the current Investigation Bureau, Legislative Bureau, Resources Bureau, Statistics Bureau, Information Committee, and part of the Budget Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, and create a Resources Bureau, Planning Bureau, and Budget Bureau, with a director-general to control these three bureaus.

(2) The second method is to establish a General Affairs Office, with the above three bureaus as its internal bureaus.

(3) The third method is to integrate the Resources Bureau and the Investigation Bureau as an agency to control important national policies.

(4) Appoint a person with the qualifications of Deputy Prime Minister as Minister without Portfolio to manage this agency.

(5) Or appoint a person with the qualifications of Chief of Staff as its director-general. (Kyodo News, December 12)

The Japanese Government Has Financial Difficulties and Is Unable to Pay for the South Manchuria Railway Shares: The Military Believes It Affects the Policy Towards Manchuria: Development of the Puppet State Budget is 1.5 Billion Yuan 70

(Tokyo) Sasaki, the director of the South Manchuria Railway Company, came to Tokyo the other day to request the government to pay the unpaid installments of all its shares. The Ministry of Finance is still considering this due to financial difficulties. However, the military believes that the government should pay the money immediately to implement the policy towards Manchuria, that is, investing in Manchuria is one of the important national policies of the government. Minister of Finance Baba is also strongly promoting the development of Manchurian industries, so appropriate methods should be considered as soon as possible. It is said that the Ministry of Finance is now refusing to pay the money, which is very unreasonable. The South Manchuria Railway Company is a national policy company with both government and private capital. Its business is the government's national policy. The government must immediately find a way to enable the South Manchuria Railway to implement its business plan. (Kyodo News, December 12)

(Changchun) The five-year plan for the development of Manchurian industries, which will begin next year, has an estimated budget of 1.5 billion yuan. The funds, in addition to issuing domestic debt, can only rely on Japan's investment in Manchuria. The mobilization of funds required is as follows: (1) The government, in addition to issuing a minimum of 300 million yuan of domestic and foreign debt, hopes to set new taxes, increase official industry income and natural income, and raise a total of 500 million yuan. (2) The South Manchuria Railway Company will be solely responsible for transportation, railways, coal and other heavy industries of 500 million yuan. (3) Private investment from mainland Japan in various industries will be 300 million yuan. (4) New financial institutions will be established, and funds of 200 million yuan can be raised by issuing bonds and mobilizing deposits. As for the industrial and transportation aspects of this plan, pure official operations and special company capital increases, or new establishments, will await government, South Manchuria Railway, and Japanese private investment. As for the agricultural and animal husbandry aspects, the dualistic guidance of the government and the South Manchuria Railway will be changed. Encouragement will be given to follow the direction of the five-year plan. Under the guidance of the government, the South Manchuria Railway will provide technical assistance and engage in developing agriculture and increasing livestock production. (Domei News Agency, December 12)

(Dalian) The "Manchukuo" government is now raising 150 million yen each in domestic and foreign debt in order to implement the five-year plan for industrial development, and has decided to levy income tax on salaried employees. It has not yet been announced when this tax will be levied. It will probably be within two years. This income will be very considerable. It is estimated that the total annual income of salaried employees in Manchuria (including the Kwantung Leased Territory) is no less than 250 million yuan. It is now believed that when this tax is levied in the future, foreigners residing in Manchuria will also have to pay this tax. (Reuters, December 12)

Double Tenth Festival in Germany 74

(Berlin) The closeness of Sino-German relations in recent years and the German people's strong interest in China can be seen at the celebration of the 25th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China held by Ambassador Cheng at the International House last night. There were hundreds of German celebrities attending, including former Minister to Peiping Erdmannsdorff, Department Chief Lahlmann of the National Socialist Party in China, Dr. Linde, Vice Chairman of the Far East Association, Admiral Lietzmann, Chairman of the Chinese Academic Research Society, Former Minister to Peiping and current President of the Frankfurt Chinese Society Pochlo, as well as many representatives from the German Ministry of Defense and the Law School. The celebration was hosted by the Chinese Students Association in Germany and the German Geological Society. In the evening, General Foppel, Chairman of the German Geological Society, delivered a welcome speech, followed by a speech by Chinese Ambassador Cheng Tianfang. Cheng pointed out the similarities between China and Germany in political development. Ambassador Cheng said that when the Republic of China was founded twenty-five years ago, some people were skeptical, saying that it was doubtful whether this ancient nation, which had been subject to thousands of years of autocratic monarchy, could implement democracy. However, twenty-five years of experience have proved that the foundation of the Republic of China is indeed built on a great stone. He also said, "The progress of Chinese politics is like the growth of human beings. Childhood has passed, and we have entered adolescence. Therefore, we have great hope for the future of China." At this point, Ambassador Cheng presented a national flag to the Mayor of Berlin, Lippert, as a souvenir. In his reply, Lippert said that the Chinese national flag and the German one both symbolize national ideals and were determined by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. He also said, "I hereby assure the Chinese Ambassador and the Chinese people with sincerity that this Chinese national flag will always occupy a glorious place in the International House." (National News Agency, November 11)

Seoul: The Korean Army Headquarters announced that on the 11th, the "Manchukuo" border surveillance team and the Soviet border police had a conflict in two places on the Soviet-Manchurian border in Jiandao Province. The main points are as follows:

(1) At 5:30 a.m. on the 11th, while a detachment of the "Manchukuo" border surveillance team was monitoring the border near Jiusha Ping in Yangguan Ping, across the river from Gucheng, that is, near the Soviet-Manchurian border, they were suddenly shot at by the Soviet border police. The surveillance team resisted and returned fire. One person was injured. The Soviet side also suffered considerable damage, abandoning a total of eight dead and wounded in Manchurian territory. At present, both the Soviet and Manchurian sides have increased their troops, and their surveillance posts are confronting the Soviet troops in Yangguan Ping and the barracks. The distance between them is 500 meters.

(2) On the afternoon of the 11th, near the 12th marker on the border line southeast of Madida, while the Manchurian border surveillance team was monitoring the border, they were suddenly shot at by the Soviet army. One member of the surveillance team was killed in action. The damage to the Soviet army is unknown. The fighting between the two sides has stopped since 5:30 p.m. on the 11th. The two sides are waiting in formation with the border line separating them by 200 meters.

(3) The Japanese army is taking comprehensive countermeasures. (Kyodo News, December 12)

British-Australian Flight: New Zealand Woman Sets New Record 76

Darwin Harbor: New Zealand's young female aviator, Ms. Batten, flew into here at 1:13 this morning, setting a solo flight record from Britain to Australia, covering the entire journey in five days, twenty-two hours and two minutes. When the lady landed, because the aircraft had an accident, after rapidly circling the field once, it stopped immediately. The audience nearby were all alarmed and at a loss, but Ms. Batten still had a smile on her face when she got off the plane, without any sign of panic, and said that she was very pleased to be able to break the previous solo flight record by 24 hours. She now intends to continue flying back to her hometown in New Zealand. This wish may be difficult to realize, because the Melbourne Civil Aviation Association opposes single-engine aircraft flying across the thousand-mile Tasman Sea. Ms. Batten took off from Lympne airfield in Kent, England, early last Monday, intending to shorten the record she had previously set from Britain to Australia. Unexpectedly, Ms. Batten made an amazing improvement, breaking the previous solo flight record by almost a full day. The highest solo flight record between Britain and Australia was held by Broadbent, with a time of six days, twenty-one hours and nineteen minutes. The flight record between Britain and Australia made by Batten herself in May 1934 was fourteen days and twenty-three hours. The aircraft she is piloting this time is the one she used to cross the South Atlantic from Dakar to Brazil in November 1935. (Reuters, December 12)

Manila: There has been a typhoon along the coast of the Philippines for several days. Twenty cities in the provinces of Benguet South, Tarlac and Nueva Ecija have been the most severely affected. Achievements of Arctic Navigation 78

(Moscow) The Arctic navigation season this year has come to a successful conclusion. The number of ships navigating the Northern Sea Route throughout the season has doubled compared to last year. Although there was a lot of ice this year, making navigation difficult, all ships were able to reach their destinations completely, and no ships stayed in the Arctic to overwinter. Water transport in the Kara Sea was also very successful. Many foreign ships also participated in the navigation. During this season, the icebreaker "Rusanov" sailed to the northernmost tip of Franz Josef Land twice in one season. The journey was very difficult. The results of this season's navigation have shown that the Northern Sea Route can be used regularly under any ice conditions. In the future, cargo transport in northern Soviet Union will increase year by year. The vast economic development of the Yakut Republic, the prosperity of industry in the Kolyma region, and the economic and cultural development of the entire northern coast of the Soviet Union will greatly increase transportation next year. Next year, the route will add many powerful new icebreakers, which are currently under construction. (TASS, December 9)

Jerusalem – The general strike throughout the region is scheduled to end today. City residents gathered in various churches yesterday to hold special prayers of thanksgiving to God. This morning, church bells rang loudly, expressing joy. The decision to end the strike was made on Saturday and Sunday after three meetings of the Arab Higher Committee and the local Arab National Committee. At that time, it was unanimously decided to accept the joint appeal letters from King Ibn Saud of Hejaz, King Abdullah of Transjordan, and King Ghazi of Iraq. Many illegal incidents have occurred in the past 24 hours. The British army barracks in Bethlehem were also shot at. British soldiers returned fire, killing two Arabs. On Friday night, Arabs attacked a convoy of armored vehicles south of Jerusalem, injuring three British soldiers and one British patrol officer. The authorities ordered the town of Hebron to pay a collective fine of £1,000 as a punitive measure. (Reuters Dispatch, 12th)

Jerusalem – Arabs in Palestine have resumed work today after a six-month strike. The doors of shops have been opened, for the first time since spring. Streetcars of Arab companies have resumed operation. However, violence has not completely stopped. There are still sniper incidents in Jewish residential areas. Last night, a Jewish policeman was shot and killed. (Reuters Dispatch, 12th)

Jerusalem – The Arab people in Palestine, due to their opposition to Jewish immigration, have been on strike since April this year, for almost half a year. Recently, after mediation by the kings of four Arab countries, Hejaz, Yemen, Iraq, and Transjordan, the Arab Higher Committee here decided yesterday to end the strike. The tribe's newspapers recently commented on this matter, all celebrating "the victory of the strike movement." The Jewish newspapers said that the government had not accepted any of the requests made by the Arab tribe, which showed that the tribe's actions had failed. However, it is generally believed that the kings of the countries must have provided some kind of promise to the Arabs here, which led to the success of the mediation. All stores run by Arabs in Jerusalem and the port of Haifa have reopened today. Construction projects that had been suspended for six months have also been resumed. The atmosphere is renewed. However, the long period of unrest and economic decline is regrettable for everyone. (Havas Dispatch, 13th)

(London) – Authorities estimate that the general strike in Palestine has resulted in the deaths of 300 people and injuries to over 1,000. It has now been announced that the strike has ended. British newspapers are delighted by this news and praise the success of the three Arab kings' mediation, as well as the British army commander in Palestine, Lieutenant General Dill, for not resorting to force lightly during the negotiations. According to British government announcements, fairness is paramount, and the three Arab kings have expressed their trust in the British government's goodwill. Commentators are echoing this view, but ignore the fact that British goodwill must be supported by concessions and compromises from both sides in Palestine in order to be effective. As the "Morning Post" stated, the policies implemented by the Palestine Mandate government have never been able to create peace and may need to be greatly modified based on their results. The "Daily News" stated that while the mandate may be able to maintain order when the Jewish and Arab nations are at odds, it will ultimately not be able to create peace and prosperity. (Reuters Dispatch, 13th)

French Prime Minister's Speech: Achievements of the Socialist Government; Financial Reform Increases National Income; General Affairs Target the Entire Working Class 82

Lens – Prime Minister Léon Blum came here today to attend the opening ceremony of a new hospital. In short, all the measures we have taken are aimed at increasing national income and the purchasing power of the masses." Regarding domestic affairs, Léon Blum said, "The main characteristic of the Popular Front government is to seek lasting cooperation with the masses and local professional organizations, because only local professional organizations can truly represent public opinion." The Prime Minister expressed optimism about the near future of the Popular Front, saying that the unity of the Popular Front is stronger than ever before. The Prime Minister continued to describe the achievements of the government in reforming general affairs, saying that among the various reform plans, the most difficult to implement was the law on a 40-hour work week. This law will be implemented first in various coal mines on November 1, and then gradually extended to the metallurgical, textile, and construction industries. The Prime Minister also said, "Once the two houses of parliament reconvene, we will quickly implement the tax reform plan. If you learn about the various measures planned by Finance Minister Olivoir, you will know that the government is by no means indecisive and tolerant. Moreover, the current experiment of the government is an experiment for the entire working class. To what extent the ideas of the working class affect the current political and social system will be determined by this experiment. As for those who regard the workers as a privileged class in society, their intention is to make the interests of workers and farmers mutually opposed. This kind of propaganda must be opposed, because if workers and farmers are opposed to each other, reactionary forces will inevitably seize the opportunity to make a comeback. The historical facts of the Second Republic in France from 1848 to 1851 are a sufficient lesson." Léon Blum reiterated various social reform policies, saying, "The government's proposed method of resolving labor-capital disputes through compulsory arbitration is actually beneficial to employers. Now, the employees have accepted it, but the employers have uniquely opposed it, which is quite incomprehensible. If it is said that employers must want to instigate internal social conflicts, or even want to restore the long-abandoned doctrine of employer supremacy, I really cannot believe it. If so, we will never be able to allow it, because the government enforces the law strictly, and once reform plans are promulgated, there is no possibility of reversing the decision." In conclusion, he said, "What I believe in and adhere to is only democracy, peace, and human dignity, only social justice. In order to realize social justice, I will do my best." (Havas News Agency Telegram, 11th)

British and French Party Disputes 83

(London) – Communist Party members paraded through the East End of London today, expressing opposition to fascism and celebrating Sunday's victory. Fascist Party members also paraded in Liverpool. No major disturbances occurred at either demonstration, with only a few people injured and several arrested for minor clashes. However, by the evening, hundreds of young people in the East End of London suddenly smashed the glass windows of fifteen shops owned by Jews in Ridell Street and looted the goods of several shops. By the time the police arrived at the scene in a public bus after hearing the alarm, the rioters had disappeared without a trace. A total of 5,000 men and women participated in today's Communist Party parade, led by 500 veterans, followed by 2,000 police officers and mounted police. Starting from the tower factory, they went to Victoria Park. A large number of police officers were lined up along the road, and the audience blocked the road. The military band played the Communist Party marching song, and the demonstrating party members sang left-wing songs and shouted slogans to defeat Mosley (leader of the British Fascist Party) and his black-shirted thugs. The demonstration by Fascist Party members in Liverpool kept the local police even busier. Although there were hundreds of police officers and mounted police protecting them on all sides as they marched, anti-fascists threw sharp objects at them. The police had no choice but to use batons to disperse the crowds. (Reuters Telegram, 11th)

Submarine Warfare: Italy Agrees to Join with Restrictions 84

(London) – After the 1930 London Naval Treaty was signed by the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan, France and Italy did not sign to join it. However, France has stated that if Italy accepts the restrictions in Part IV of the treaty (i.e., the part concerning submarine warfare), France will also sign to join it. It has been heard that Italy will formally join this part. Once the country implements its accession, the terms contained in Part IV of the treaty will take effect. (Havas Dispatch, 12th)

Opposition to Nationalizing British Armaments 85

(London) – The Cabinet previously appointed a special committee on armaments manufacturing to study the issue of nationalizing the armaments industry. Well-informed sources have recently announced that the committee has submitted a report opposing the proposal for nationalization. There are three reasons for this: (1) This move would cause the government to waste huge sums of money to strengthen armaments, but it may not be effective in national defense. (2) This move would force the government to constantly hire a huge number of workers, who may even receive salaries for doing nothing. (3) This move would allow the arms industry to be controlled by the political situation and not maintain its independent nature. In addition, the committee advocates that in times of war, the government should absolutely control the armaments industry and mobilize capital to meet emergency needs. However, in peacetime, the following system may be adopted: (1) The government may recognize the armaments industry as a public utility and control it within a considerable scope. (2) When foreign countries order armaments from British factories, the government agencies should investigate the quantity ordered and the transaction price, so as to avoid the factories from obtaining excessive profits. (3) The laws on merchants applying for armaments export licenses should be strictly revised, so that the government can implement various supervision methods, such as refusing to supply armaments to semi-civilized countries. (Havas Dispatch, 12th)

Actions Toward Chahar and Suiyuan After the Jiabusi Conference; Mongol Bandits and Puppet Troops All Receive Assistance; The Situation in the Five Counties East of Suiyuan Becomes Increasingly Serious 90

His troops consist of two cavalry brigades, one infantry brigade, and one special service regiment, totaling over 5,500 men. The seriousness of the situation in the five counties east of Suiyuan is feared to escalate as a result. The conference in Jiabusi, for the situation of Chahar north and Suiyuan east, does not belong to a simple, local problem, but the expansion of its background involves the entire national policy, which makes the conference in Jiabusi extremely important. It is now learned that the conference concluded on the 7th of this month, and the military and political leaders of various bandits and puppets have all returned to their original stationed locations. The important discussions at the conference were the decision on the timing of the invasion of eastern Suiyuan (i.e., the five counties east of Suiyuan), and it has been resolved to gradually increase the military strength on the border between Chahar and Suiyuan from today, advancing westward in stages. As for the salaries and supplies of the puppet bandit troops, a small portion of it depends on the local collection of autumn taxes and other miscellaneous levies. Shantou Japanese Residents' Demands Regarding the Abandoned Bomb Case; Shantou Military and Police Still Not Relaxing Vigilance; Smuggled Drugs Mailed to Shantou 91

Shantou Correspondence: Shantou is a vital hub for the Japanese's southward advance policy. After the peaceful unification of Guangdong, the Guangzhi Foreign Firm abandoned bomb case occurred. It is said that this incident involved some clever and illusory tactics. For example, last year, a Japanese patrolman named Kakuda died suddenly in Lianhe Lane in Shantou. After examination by a British doctor at the Gospel Hospital, it was confirmed that the deceased's lungs had already rotted and there was no hope of prolonging his life. However, the Japanese side claimed that Kakuda was shot by a sniper. There were many suspicious points, and it remains an unsolved case to this day. Therefore, the Guangzhi Foreign Firm incident may also involve clever and illusory tactics. However, the Japanese merchants in Shantou have adopted an unusually strong stance regarding the Guangzhi Foreign Firm incident. Through a resolution by the Japanese Residents' Association, two points were decided: (1) Strictly arrest the murderers and protect Japanese residents; (2) Guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future, and incidentally expand the authority of the Japanese police. This was submitted to the city government by Japanese Consul Yamazaki for negotiation. The city government previously sent Huang Jing, a councilor, along with Xiong Jixia, the head of the detective section of the Public Security Bureau, to the Japanese Consulate to repeatedly investigate the origin of the abandoned bomb with Kita, the head of the Japanese police station. They believed there were many points of suspicion, so they did not reply. However, heavily armed military police in Shantou have been stationed in double shifts since the evening of the 17th of last month and have still not relaxed vigilance. On the morning of the 3rd of this month, Kita, the head of the Japanese police, accompanied by an interpreter, visited the Inspectorate of the Public Security Bureau to inquire about the measures taken by Inspector Lian Bingyi regarding the abandoned bomb case and the procedures for Japanese residents to rent houses in Shantou. Lian said that the occurrence of the abandoned bomb was only based on one-sided reports, and there was no evidence to prove that it was thrown from the outside. Because the bomb had no firing pin and was a discarded item from ten years ago, and it was found under the kitchen, and the back door and windows were tightly closed, and the guards did not see anyone passing by, there was no basis to prove that it was thrown by someone. As for the issue of foreigners renting houses, the city government will have proper measures soon, etc. Kita left without getting the information he wanted. It is noted that the Japanese's infiltration and activities for their southward advance have been very remarkable recently in several aspects. The year before last, the Japanese established the "Combination Company" in Shantou and "Tonghe" in Hong Kong, specializing in the import of foreign rice and goods with special agricultural taxes. In two years, they made a profit of one million yuan, which greatly impacted the transportation guilds and sundry goods businesses in the north and south ports. The power over grain and foreign trade in Chaozhou and Meizhou was almost entirely in the hands of the Combination Company. After the Guangdong situation was settled, the foreign rice tax was collected by the customs, and the Combination Company was also suspended. Recently, because the Agricultural Tax Bureau has not issued a clear order to cancel, heavy taxes are still levied on soybeans, oil, bean cakes, coconut oil, and miscellaneous grains. Relying on commercial treaties, the Japanese refuse to pay local taxes after reporting to the customs. Last month, the Combination Company was revived, managed by Japanese man Takaji Saburo, who entrusted the Northeast Mitsubishi Corporation to handle the import of oil, soybeans, peanut kernels, etc., making a huge profit. The old shareholders demanded to join, and later, under the guidance and mediation of the Taiwan Development Company of Taiwan, the organization was expanded and renamed the Zhongnan Company, with even more substantial capital than before. Many foreign houses along the coast of Shantou's outer road have been rented at high prices by Taiwanese people through intermediaries, and foreign firm signboards have been hung up, specializing in high-profit businesses. Anything that the Japanese and Koreans operate in Tianjin and Beijing is beginning to take shape in Shantou, such as hotels, bars, and cafes, which are the only gold-consuming dens when smoking and gambling are prohibited. Dancing girls and drugs are active secretly at the same time. The Shantou General Post Office has been receiving a large number of packages containing rayon and pharmaceuticals from Tianjin, Beijing, and Xiamen in recent days. Drugs are hidden in the middle, and the package surfaces are written with the names of certain foreign firms. Postmen have searched all over the city, but no such foreign firm signboards can be found, so they cannot be delivered. However, every two or three days, someone brings a slip and the foreign firm's seal to collect them. Some packages are even sent to small post offices not far from Shantou, which also cannot be delivered. Within two days, someone also comes with a seal to collect them. The purpose is nothing more than to avoid various local taxes, special taxes, and customs inspections. The inflow of drugs also comes from these packages, which is enough to show the deep intentions of a certain country.

Guangdong Province Begins to Rectify Salt Affairs; Transportation Office and Audit Office Merged; Plans to Restore Sales Markets in Hunan Province 92

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has always been known for its salt production. In its heyday, Guangdong salt was sold to provinces such as Guangxi, Guizhou, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Fujian. Most salt-producing areas are located in coastal regions. The most productive areas along the East River are Haifeng, Lufeng, Shanwei, and Huiyang. The most famous salt areas in the Southern Route are Gaolei, Qinlian, and Qiongya. In the past decade, the sales markets in various provinces have gradually been lost. For example, Jiangxi Province has suffered from communist disasters for several years, and the official army has blockaded southern Jiangxi, cutting off the road for Guangdong salt to be sold to Jiangxi. In the northern part of Hunan Province, the import of Huai salt has occurred, while in southern Hunan, heavy salt taxes are levied upon entry, making it impossible for Guangdong salt to sell smoothly. As for Guangxi Province, there has recently been an influx of Vietnamese salt, which is cheap, making it impossible for Guangdong salt to compete. As a result, the road for Guangdong salt to be sold to Guangxi is not as good as before. Due to the above reasons, the export of Guangdong salt has plummeted. In addition, those who have been in charge of salt administration in recent years have lacked long-term plans and only pursued personal gain, leading to the relaxation of salt administration. As a result, Guangdong's salt affairs have become increasingly weakened, leading to the bankruptcy of salt merchants and affecting other commercial industries. In recent years, Guangdong's salt affairs have been in a desperate situation. Recently, the Guangdong situation has been renewed. Chen Weizhou, the Liangguang Salt Transport Commissioner, has left office. The central government then appointed Tang Haian as his successor. Before long, Tang also left office, and the central government appointed Tang Dong, the manager of the Guangdong Salt Affairs Audit Sub-Office, to serve concurrently as the Liangguang Salt Transport Commissioner. Tang took office on the 5th of this month and was ordered to thoroughly reform the administrative, sales, and anti-smuggling matters within the office. To save public funds, he will reduce staff and merge the Transport Commissioner's Office with the Audit Sub-Office. The monthly expenses of the Transport Commissioner's Office were formerly 80,000 to 90,000 yuan, but now they have been reduced to 8,000 yuan per month. The magistrates of salt fields in various places will also be dismissed, and administrative matters will be handled concurrently by the tax collection offices. The above are administrative reforms. As for anti-smuggling, the entire province will be divided into six to eight anti-smuggling zones, with a tax police team stationed in each zone. The original salt police general team will be dissolved to unify anti-smuggling powers. It has also been decided to send personnel to the salt fields to reorganize them. One method of reorganization is to improve salt quality. The office will send inspection experts to various fields to study and guide them. There are fifteen salt field districts in Guangdong, with varying amounts and qualities of salt. The main salt fields, such as Bobai, Sanya, and Wushi, are planned to be reorganized first. Secondary salt fields, such as Shiqiao, Danshui, Dazhou, Biga, Dianmao, Bomao, Shuang'en, Baishi, and Haishan, will be reorganized and smuggling will be prevented. Salt fields that are not very important, such as Zhaolong, will be abolished. As for improving transportation and sales, it is planned to first build salt warehouses in various places, gradually abolish Cheng boats, and abolish the restriction of evenly distributing 30% to eastern and 70% to western fields, implementing a free transportation and sales system. Sales methods have been discussed with salt merchants in southern Hunan to restore the method of transporting and selling Guangdong salt to thirty-eight counties in southern Hunan. It is also planned to first build salt warehouses in various places in the Southern Route to facilitate the loading, unloading, and storage of salt. As for the Cheng boats used to transport salt, it is still difficult to abolish them all at once. There are currently over a hundred of these Cheng boats. The largest can carry 8,000 bags of salt, while the smallest can carry over 2,400 bags. Each boat employs an average of twenty workers, totaling over 2,000 people who make a living on the salt boats. If the boats are abolished all at once, over 2,000 people will lose their jobs. Therefore, a gradual reform plan is proposed, with fifteen Cheng boats being abolished each year, with the aim of completing the abolition in five years to avoid sudden unemployment for the workers. (October 9th)

Qingdao Cracks Down on Counterfeit Subsidiary Coin Manufacturing Organization; Counterfeiters Xiao Ziyu and Four Others Arrested; All Machinery and Counterfeit Coins Seized 93

Qingdao Correspondence: Recently, there has been a shortage of nickel-quality subsidiary coins on the market, and there have been many counterfeit coins, which are difficult to identify. If strict precautions are not taken, the impact on the national currency and the disruption of finance will be significant. Recently, the city cracked down on a counterfeit banknote manufacturing organization. Yesterday (the 11th), the Public Security Bureau cracked down on a counterfeit subsidiary coin manufacturing organization in Wujiacun, outside the city, and arrested the suspects and seized the evidence on the spot. Xiao Ziyu (45 years old), a native of Jimo, lives at No. 303, Xiwujiacun, outside the city. He used to run a coal mine in Taiping Town. However, since the past year, the market has been depressed, and all industries have been sluggish. Xiao's coal mine has also been greatly affected and cannot be maintained. Therefore, he came up with a whimsical idea and discussed with his friend Li Baoqing and others to raise funds to manufacture counterfeit subsidiary coins in the hope of making a profit. Xiao and Li each contributed 100 yuan as capital, and Xiao found ways to purchase machinery and modeling equipment. To maintain strict secrecy, two rooms were rented at No. 303, Xiwujiacun, outside the city, as a temporary manufacturing plant, and two coppersmiths, Wang Qisheng and Zhang Kequan, were hired to start manufacturing. Zheng Zhibin was hired as a salesman, and a price was set: 40 yuan of legal tender for every 100 yuan of counterfeit subsidiary coins.

A line vendor named Yu ordered 100 yuan of counterfeit subsidiary coins from Zheng and asked Zheng to deliver them to the woods at Haipobridge for exchange. Yesterday (the 11th) at about 11:00 AM, Zheng brought 500 pieces of 20-cent counterfeit subsidiary coins to deliver the goods. When he arrived near Haipobridge, his hurried behavior and abnormal demeanor were noticed by patrol police officers, who immediately searched him. 500 counterfeit subsidiary coins were found on his person, and Zheng was taken to the Fourth Bureau of Public Security for interrogation. Zheng initially denied it cunningly and refused to confess. However, as the evidence was conclusive, he could not deny it and fully confessed the counterfeit subsidiary coin manufacturing organization and his accomplices. The Fourth Bureau sent a patrol officer, Meng Dexuan, and several long-term police officers to search No. 303, Caiyuan, Wujiacun. The suspects Xiao Ziyu, Li Baoqing, Wang Qisheng, and Zhang Kequan were all arrested, and several counterfeit subsidiary coins and counterfeit subsidiary coin manufacturing machines were seized. They were all taken back to the branch for interrogation. Xiao Ziyu and others have confessed without denial. The Fourth Bureau sent all the suspects to the General Bureau on the 12th, and they will be severely punished according to the law to serve as a warning to others.

The Zhejiang Provincial Silk Control Association issued approximately 900,000 sheets of improved silkworm eggs this fall. The feeding process went very well. However, due to sudden changes in the silkworms during the spinning period, the harvest was reduced. The purchase of autumn cocoons has now been concluded, totaling about 100,000 dan. 90,000 sheets of late-autumn silkworm eggs have also been distributed, and the cocoon harvest can also be completed by the end of this month. The autumn silkworm affairs have come to an end.

Zhejiang Sea Fishing Season Flourishing

Since the large pair fishing boats in Dinghai Shenjiamen were launched in early August of the lunar calendar, they have reached three to four hundred pairs. The harvest of each wind is also quite considerable. In recent days, the average harvest of the ships docking in the port is five to six hundred catties. At the lowest price, each pair can earn thirty to forty yuan. According to the survey, the earliest fishing boats to be launched have earned six to seven hundred yuan in the past half month, while the smaller ones have also earned three to four hundred yuan. If the harvest can be maintained as such in the second half of the year, the economy of the fishing village will be easy to restore. In addition, more than a hundred large pair boats from Yindong Hubang arrived in Shenjiamen on the 8th, making the local market suddenly lively.

Taizhou 104

Capture of Chopping Knife Society Leader

According to a report from Wu ErMei, a farmer in Shiqiao Town, Wenling County, the leaders of the Chopping Knife Society, Jiang Sanya, Jiang Mingdong, and Jiang Xiaodou, are rampant in the countryside, arbitrarily extorting money from the people, requesting their arrest to maintain local security. The county government immediately secretly ordered Squad Leader Zhao of the Police Brigade to lead soldiers in disguise to arrest the three criminals at their addresses and sent them to the county government for investigation on the 5th.

Yuyao 105

Zhejiang East Aos Restores Weighing and Releasing

The Zhejiang East Aos refused to accept the fixed amount of salt for a month. The Transportation Office tried its best to mediate, but because the Garrison Commissioner did not agree to the inner feelings, the matter almost changed. Later, the Transportation Office telegraphed the Left Changzhang to be responsible for the dredging, and severely ordered the Zhejiang East Aos to open the collection within a limited time to avoid triggering an incident. The Left Changzhang mediated and negotiated a compromise, and the representatives of both parties signed it. The Zhejiang East Aos also restored the weighing and releasing from the 1st, and the salt tide that had been in dispute for nine months was completely resolved. The method is: (1) The salt farmers' annual salt production per plate is 381 catties, and the Aos merchants will temporarily buy 300 catties. The remaining 81 catties will still be stored with the salt farmers, and will be weighed and released again when the sales improve. (2) The salt sold by the Aos merchants should first sell the salt received by this decision. In the future, if the sales are completed, the remaining salt stored by the Aos merchants and salt farmers will continue to be sold in half to maintain the livelihood of the salt farmers. (3) Remit 80,000 yuan to Yuyao first, and the salt farmers will be paid four corners of ocean per piece as a living maintenance fee.

City Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Requesting Correction of Customs' Discriminatory Treatment of Chinese Merchants 107

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, regarding the matter of the Shanghai Motor Silk Weaving Factory Association's letter of the 9th of this month, which states that its member, the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, has reported that the Jianghai Customs regulations stipulate that for all import and export customs declarations, the name of the declaring company or firm, as well as the name of the manager, must be registered with the customs in advance. This is uniformly applied to both Chinese and foreign merchants. However, for Chinese citizens, it is also necessary to submit a photograph of the manager, while foreigners are not required to submit a photograph. This is discriminatory and implies a special meaning. The Jianghai Customs is the Customs of the Republic of China, and customs administration has long been reclaimed as autonomous. However, this old habit of discriminating against Chinese people has not yet been abolished. This is not only unequal treatment but also makes people feel inferior. Therefore, we dare to request your association to forward the situation to the Ministry of Finance, the Customs Administration, and the Inspector General of Customs, requesting them to order corrections. For Chinese customs declaration registration, it should also be treated the same as foreigners, without the need to submit photographs. If it is believed that Chinese people's English signatures are not always completely identical, then either Chinese signatures or seals can be used, which should be accurate and reliable. Since the customs is the customs of China, its signatures, etc., should also be based on Chinese. We hope you will investigate and handle this matter and reply." The letter also stated that the Jianghai Customs is the Customs of the Republic of China and has long been reclaimed as autonomous. All old habits that cause inconvenience to the Chinese people and discriminate against Chinese should be renovated to promote national dignity and ensure equal treatment. According to the letter, we should respond by inquiring and requesting a forwarding. Upon arrival, the chamber found that the treatment of Chinese and foreign merchants by the customs should be uniform. It is said that when merchants register with the customs to handle customs declaration matters themselves, Chinese merchants must attach a photo of the manager, while foreign merchants do not have this procedure. Such treatment clearly distinguishes between superior and inferior, which is not only contrary to the principle of fairness in government orders but also a stain on the national dignity. It is said that this measure is due to the fact that Chinese people's English signatures are not always completely identical. Therefore, the customs' measure is inherently inappropriate, as Chinese people are not inherently familiar with English signatures, and occasional discrepancies are common. In recent years, all customs documents related to Chinese citizens have mostly been changed to Chinese. Why should we still adhere to old habits for self-declaration and force the use of English signatures? Is this not forcing the difficult and subtly creating a distinction? The rights and interests of merchants regarding the treatment of taxes on machine-made foreign goods and the registration of companies or trademarks are no different in importance compared to customs declaration registration. According to past practice, these documents are based on the manager's signature and seal, and there are no errors. How can the customs create a separate standard and impose treatment on Chinese merchants that foreign merchants do not have? It is reasonable to telegraph this to your department for review and approval, and we humbly request that you immediately order all customs offices to change the registration of Chinese merchants' customs declarations to be based on the manager's Chinese signature or seal, in order to promote national dignity and show uniformity. We are most urgently awaiting your order." The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce respectfully asks.

Nissin Company Competes for River Transportation on the Yangtze 110

Two Ships Added to the Shanghai-Hankou Line; Fierce Competition on the Hankou-Yichang Route

In the downstream shipping business of the Yangtze River, besides the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Minsheng Industrial Company, which have a strong presence in transporting passengers and goods, the Japanese-owned Nissin Steamship Company also has a significant presence in the Shanghai-Hankou shipping business. Since the "September 18th" and "January 28th" incidents, the Chinese people, driven by righteous indignation, have voluntarily converted to Chinese ships, and the business of Japanese ships has slightly declined. Recently, due to the increasing congestion of Japanese goods imports, the company's original six ships, Yueyang, Nanyang, Ruiyang, Xiangyang, Luoyang, and Fengyang, which operate on the Shanghai-Hankou route, are insufficient. Therefore, starting from the Double Tenth Festival, it has specially added the Dayuan and Daji commercial ships to the Shanghai-Hankou route to compete with Chinese state-owned and private commercial ships. On the Hankou-Changsha and Hankou-Yichang routes, Nissin also has three ships, Wuling, Yuanjiang, and Dangyang, operating back and forth, fiercely competing with the Minsheng Steamship Company.

A Glimpse of the Japanese Military in the Zhabei and Hongkou Areas: Ouyang Road Outpost Removed, Military Telephone Continues to Be Repaired, Exercises in Hongkou Park 112

Although the Japanese marines in the Zhabei and Hongkou areas have not been completely withdrawn, the surface situation has indeed become quieter. The Japanese military outpost inside the Japanese Girls' School at the intersection of Ouyang Road and Sida Road has been removed. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency passed by there yesterday and saw only two Japanese soldiers on guard in front of the gate. Armored vehicles, military trucks, and motorcycles were all gone. According to reports, the area is a city garden, and nearby Qimei Road and other places are all peaceful. In the Jiangwan Road area, except for the Japanese troops at the Tongji Road intersection, who still send three or four guards three times a day in the name of protecting Japanese students, there is nothing unusual. However, at about 3:30 in the afternoon, two Japanese military trucks carrying 70 or 80 soldiers and two or three people who looked like senior officers in a car drove into the end of Huayuan Street one after another. At the same time, another eight trucks, all carrying more than 200 Japanese soldiers, departed from the Japanese Marine Corps Headquarters in Jiangwan, turned east on North Sichuan Road, and did not know where they were going. Less than half an hour later, the empty trucks returned via Dixiwei Road. Also, when the reporter passed through the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Dixiwei Road at about 9:00 am, he saw three Japanese soldiers repairing a military telephone there. There were also Japanese military exercises in Hongkou Park. However, according to the park guards, Japanese military exercises in the park have become commonplace and have not been interrupted for several days. The exercise time is always at 9:30 or 10:00, with as many as 500 or 600 people and as few as 200 or 300 people, all fully armed with machine guns and other weapons. The park has almost become a training ground for Japanese soldiers.

The Japanese military outposts in various places in Hongkou, except for the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Qiujiang Branch Road, which have been completely removed, there were three at the Jiuxing Road Bridge and two at the intersection of Laobazi Road and Wusong Road yesterday morning, which were removed in the afternoon. There were none at the intersection of Dixiwei Road and Tiantong Road yesterday morning, but there were suddenly two in the afternoon. Furthermore, the Japanese consulate has not yet responded to our city government's protest, and the Japanese military has not completely withdrawn, so it cannot be said that there are no hidden worries.

Supplementary Tax and Licensing for Accumulated Rayon Fabrics for Transportation and Sale 117

Factories Across the Country Must Handle This Uniformly, Ministry of Industry and Commerce Notified the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Weaving Association Yesterday

Regarding the smuggling of rayon fabrics from North China for sale in South China, the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Weaving United Association telegraphed the Ministry of Industry and Commerce requesting that it refuse to issue licenses for the transportation and sale of rayon fabrics from North China. Now, it has received a notice from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Commercial Character No. 48756, stating: "Regarding the association's telegram requesting the rejection of the Tianjin Dyeing and Weaving Industry representatives' petition to have the accumulated rayon fabrics issued transportation licenses by the customs, all of which should be taxed according to the same tax rate as South China, the Ministry believed that this matter concerned tax administration and consulted the Ministry of Finance for review and handling and made written instructions. Now, it has received a reply from the Ministry of Finance stating that the methods for checking and cleaning up the factory ten goods worth of rayon were previously prescribed by the Ministry. All factories should clean up according to the regulations and report that if the rayon accumulated in the customs registration cannot provide proof of tax payment, it should be taxed according to regulations. The customs will issue a transportation license for the accumulated piece goods. Factories across the country must handle this uniformly. The Ministry previously received a telegram from the Inspector General of Customs stating that the accumulated rayon and the amount of hemp yarn stored on the machines in the Tianjin City Dyeing and Weaving Industry Association's factory had been checked and found to be consistent by the Tianjin Customs. The customs had already been instructed to pay supplementary taxes on the accumulated rayon and hemp yarn stored on the machines and issue transportation licenses for the accumulated piece goods. This is handled according to the original method. After the cleanup, the customs should check the rayon used by each factory and the piece goods woven according to regulations, which can prevent the purchase of smuggled rayon as raw materials for piece goods and maintain the business of legitimate merchants." Special notice.

Director Pan Discusses the Social Affairs Bureau's Budget Reduction: Layoffs are a Matter of Funding, No Intention to Add Appointments at City Schools or Vocational Education 118

Shanghai News: After the merger and reorganization of the city's Social Affairs and Education Bureaus, a portion of the original personnel was unable to continue due to the order to economize on expenses, causing misunderstandings among outsiders who were unaware of the truth. Director Pan of the Social Affairs Bureau gave the following speech yesterday: "After the merger and reorganization of the two bureaus, I was ordered by the municipal government to reduce the regular expenses by 10,000 yuan per month. In addition to economizing on office expenses, the scope has been reduced, and staff members will inevitably be overlooked. This is a matter of funding, not a matter of people. There are those who regret being dismissed and are unwilling to understand, and some troublemakers are taking the opportunity to distribute anonymous leaflets and openly slander. They do not know that this unavoidable measure within my responsibilities was not what I wanted. I sympathize with the dismissed staff members and have not only detailed this in the letter I sent to each dismissed staff member but have also submitted a request to the municipal government to provide appropriate compensation. If the municipal government can consider being lenient with the bureau's funding, the bureau will re-employ a portion of the personnel to provide resettlement. As for my dedication to party and government affairs over the years, I am very tired. Before the merger and reorganization of the two bureaus, I briefly planned to recuperate and repeatedly petitioned the central authorities and the mayor to resign, but I was not allowed. Therefore, I am still doing my best. However, as long as I am in office, I will be responsible for the work of the Social Affairs Bureau in the future and will strive to promote it. Personnel changes are something I have always been cautious about. I have no intention of reappointing the principals and faculty of the city's schools, and I have never even thought about it. As a party member, I ask myself to cherish and protect others. If everyone can work hard within the scope of their responsibilities, I will be busy protecting them. Why would I talk about transferring them? I hope everyone can work with peace of mind, and the facts will be the most powerful proof."

Nanjing City Autumn National Goods Exhibition Solicits Exhibits by Letter 119

The Autumn National Goods Exhibition held by the Nanjing City National Goods Exhibition Hall has been scheduled to open on November 10th. At the same time, a temporary National Goods Market will be set up. Yesterday, staff were sent to Shanghai to contact various national goods organizations to participate. The letter and solicitation rules sent to each organization are recorded below.

Letter to Various Organizations

The Nanjing National Goods Exhibition Hall sends a letter to various organizations: "Respectfully, our hall holds a National Goods Exhibition every year to engage in the actual promotion of national goods, extensively soliciting the latest national products and famous specialties from all over the country for display and exhibition, in order to awaken the capital's citizens' interest in using national goods and increase their knowledge of national goods products. At the same time, during the exhibition period, a temporary National Goods Market is held, inviting national manufacturers to participate in sales, which not only facilitates visitors to purchase but also increases the effectiveness of national product promotion. Over the years, the results have been remarkable. This year, we are pleased to see that the country has a bumper harvest, and the national economy is more active. Our hall plans to take advantage of the opportunity to hold the 25th Autumn National Goods Exhibition, scheduled to open on November 10th. The exhibition period is tentatively set for 20 days. During the exhibition period, a temporary National Goods Market will be set up and various expanded publicity methods will be adopted to promote the work of promoting national goods to the fullest extent. Your association has always been enthusiastic about promoting national goods, so we are sending you this special letter, hoping that you will investigate and collect national products and send them to the hall ten days before the opening so that they can be numbered and arranged. We also hope that you will inform the national manufacturers in your area to actively participate in the temporary market sales and contribute to the grand event. We will be grateful for your public friendship. In order to expand publicity, our hall welcomes national manufacturers to set up publicity advertisements at the venue and make various performances of national goods manufacturing or effectiveness. However, the advertisements should be novel and attractive, otherwise, our hall will have the discretion to select and combine them. We are sending this together."

Solicitation Rules

Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 11 of the Nanjing City National Goods Exhibition Hall Regulations. Article 2: All exhibits collected shall be limited to national goods. The exhibitor must be a citizen of the Republic of China. Article 3: The categories of exhibits collected are as follows: (1) Agricultural and forestry products, (2) Mineral products, (3) Dyeing and weaving industry, (4) Chemical industry, (5) Machine-made products, (6) Handicrafts, (7) Educational supplies, (8) Artworks, (9) Food and beverages, (10) Medicines, (11) Industrial raw materials, (12) Fur and leather goods, (13) Aquatic and marine products, (14) Other categories. Article 4: The exhibits collected must meet the following conditions: (1) Able to be sold abroad or have the hope of being sold abroad, (2) Sold widely in the country, (3) Considered to have the value of an exhibit. Article 5: The following items shall not be collected: (1) Dangerous or easily damaged items, (2) Items that are harmful to social customs, order, or hygiene, (3) Items that are considered to have no value as an exhibit. Article 6: The quantity of goods collected is as follows: However, special goods are not limited to this: Piece goods are limited to one to three pieces per item, dozens are limited to one to three dozen per item, sets are limited to one to three sets per item, pieces are limited to one to three pieces per item, catties are limited to one to three catties per item, and measures are limited to one to three liters per item. Article 7: The hall collects exhibits in two ways: direct collection and indirect collection: (1) Direct collection is carried out by the hall sending staff to various production areas across the country to collect them together with the local governments and agricultural, industrial, and commercial organizations. However, exhibitors may also send them directly for display. (2) Indirect collection is carried out by the hall submitting a request to the Social Affairs Bureau to send letters to local governments across the country or entrusting other industrial institutions to collect them. Article 8: The exhibitor must fill out an exhibit application form, description, and exhibit catalog and send them to the hall for reference. The exhibit application form, description, and catalog format will be determined separately. Article 9: After the exhibits are sent to the hall and pass the examination, a receipt will be issued and the hall will be responsible for safekeeping. However, the hall shall not be liable for damages caused by natural disasters or force majeure. Article 10: The exhibits may be sold on consignment at the price agreed upon by the exhibitor. If the exhibition has been full for one year and has not been sold on consignment, the exhibitor may retrieve it with the original receipt or exchange it for a new product for display. Otherwise, the hall may dispose of it freely for cleaning purposes. Article 11: During the exhibition period, if the exhibitor wishes to replace the exhibits with new products, the new products must be sent to the hall for verification and receipt before the old products can be taken back. Article 12: If there are any matters not covered in these rules, they may be amended at any time with approval. Article 13: These rules shall be implemented after being approved for record.

Gathering of Foreign Warships in the Huangpu River: Japanese Vessels Most Numerous, Followed by British, French, and American 120

Since the murder of Japanese sailor Tagang, the situation in the Far East has become tense. Consequently, various countries have mobilized their Far East fleets to protect their overseas citizens. Currently, there are a total of twenty-one foreign warships berthed in the Huangpu River, setting a new record for the number of foreign warships stationed in Shanghai. Details are as follows:

France

After the Shanghai Incident occurred, the French government immediately telegraphed General Esteva, commander of the French Far East Fleet stationed in Weihaiwei, to dispatch warships to Shanghai. Upon receiving the order, General Esteva personally boarded the flagship "La Motte-Picquet" and led the gunboats "Tahr" and "Admiral Rénouart," arriving in Shanghai from Weihai on the 6th. They are all berthed on the Huangpu River off the French Concession Bund and at the naval pontoon, totaling four ships including the previously stationed "General Amiral Charner" gunboat.

United States

The United States Far East Fleet was originally stationed in the South Seas area. After receiving news of the Shanghai Incident, Admiral Maben, commander of the Far East Fleet, sailed on the flagship "Augusta," leading the gunboat "Asheville" and the "Trenton" cruiser, arriving in Shanghai on the 1st of this month. Including the cruiser "Milwaukee," which arrived last month, there are a total of four warships stationed.

Great Britain

In addition to the existing British warship "Peterel" stationed in Shanghai, Rear Admiral Leatham, commander of the British China Fleet, dispatched the destroyer "Grafton" to Shanghai and personally came to Shanghai on the flagship "Kent" for inspection. Now that the situation in Shanghai has returned to normal, it is scheduled to sail south within days. As for the two Italian warships originally stationed in Shanghai to protect their citizens, now that the situation in Shanghai has gradually eased, except for the gunboat "Lepanto" stationed in Shanghai, the other gunboat "Ermanno Carlotto" has already gone to Hankou.

Japan

Vice Admiral Oikawa, commander of the Japanese Third Fleet, is usually stationed in Shanghai. Therefore, there are more Japanese warships stationed in Shanghai than those of other countries. However, since the Tagang murder case, in addition to sending naval landing forces for defense, warships stationed in various locations have also been ordered to come to Shanghai to provide support. However, they mainly transported landing forces and ammunition, so they returned immediately after arriving in Shanghai. A total of two ships have made round trips. Currently in Shanghai are four ships: the flagship Izumo, the cruiser Tatsuta, the destroyer Satsuki, the destroyers Nagatsuki and Minazuki, five torpedo boats, a transport ship, and one gunboat.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Tea Association: Group Review of Proposals Yesterday, General Meeting to Be Held This Morning to Pass Resolutions, Amend Articles of Association, and Elect Additional Directors 121

After the opening of the first annual meeting of the Chinese Tea Association, the meeting was divided into four groups yesterday morning—General Affairs, Production, Transportation and Sales, and Other—to review the proposals. The report was completed in the evening, and a general meeting is scheduled to continue at the Huzhou Guild Hall on Guizhou Road at 9:00 this morning. After the proposals are passed, the meeting will be adjourned. Details are as follows:

Review Meeting

At the first general meeting the day before yesterday, it was decided to divide into four groups—General Affairs, Production, Transportation and Sales, and Other—to recommend committee members to review more than 180 proposals related to improving the production and sales of the entire tea industry. Yesterday: (1) The General Affairs Group was convened by Wang Zhenhuan and Yu Xiji, address: Yangzhuang Tea Trade Association, Gujia Lane; (2) The Production Group was convened by Fang Hanzhou and Peng Zhiqian, address: Oriental Tea Shop, Yu Qiaqing Road; (3) The Transportation and Sales Group was convened by Yu Fu and Lin Yaoting, address: Yangzhuang Tea Trade Association, Gujia Lane; (4) The Other Group (i.e., Miscellaneous Affairs Group) was convened by Tang Jishan and Ning Weiting, address: Huafu Company, Tianjin Road. All four groups began their review at 9:00 a.m., combining relevant proposals. By 6:00 p.m., all were completed and submitted to the Commodity Inspection Bureau, where the association staff member Fan Hejun compiled and mimeographed them for distribution to the members.

Proposal Report

The main points of the proposals after deliberation are recorded as follows:

(A) General Affairs Group: (1) Proposals for improving general affairs and uniting to protect interests; (2) Proposal for establishing a Tea Association Fund Committee; (3) Proposals for enriching the association's organization and tasks; (4) Proposal for electing staff to reside at the association and preside over general affairs; (5) The association should suggest to the government its responsibility for tea industry construction; (6) Proposal for widely soliciting members; (7) Proposal for publishing publications to promote propaganda; (8) Proposal for compiling a series of tea industry books; (B) Production Group: (1) Proposal for encouraging the national tea industry production; (2) Tea seedlings should be added to the nurseries in each county; (3) Proposal for establishing tea machinery factories; (4) Please ask the government and tea area public groups to supervise, encourage, reward, and subsidize tea farmers to implement production improvements; (5) Green tea should be stored in warehouses; (6) Organize school tea gardens; (7) Request the government to set standard tea prices and prohibit competing sales and auctions for compliance; (10) Suggest that the government's tea industry cooperation should focus on raw tea cooperation; (11) To change the Qihong transportation and sales cooperation, it is proposed to change to fresh leaf primary processing cooperation; (12) Black tea raw tea should be made by tea farmers themselves; (13) Correct the abuses of early picking; (14) Reform the tea stoves in the Ping Shui tea area; (16) Please organize tea cooperation improvement zones; (17) Sales emergency improvement; (18) The purchase of raw materials for making black tea should adopt the Sichuan raw material grading system; (19) Zhejiang Province plans to manage Ping Shui tea transportation and sales in the tea field; (10) Please suggest that the government control brick tea production and sales; (21) The government's tea industry control should start with improving the origin manufacturing; (22) It is to guide the establishment of primary processing cooperatives for black tea production; (23) Please order the government to supervise tea improvement in a group system and provide technical and economic assistance; (24) Request the government to establish a national tea industry improvement site; (25) Request the government to allocate funds to improve West Lake tea; (26) Exported tea should be manufactured according to standard quality; (27) Request to limit picking to avoid oversupply and impede sales; (28) Please ask the government to organize a tea cargo silver group to handle all tea industry loans; (29) Adopt a systematic organization method for foreign-owned tea making in Wenzhou to consolidate capital enrichment; (C) Transportation and Sales Group: (1) Organize a Chinese tea transportation and sales cooperative; (2) Request assistance in effectively prohibiting "returned soul tea" to emphasize citizen health; (3) Formulate standard sample opening, determine annual box export quota, unify weighing and silver collection to eliminate malpractices; (4) Suggest that the government ban rebates from Hangzhou tea shops; (5) Request that the government postpone the implementation of control over foreign-owned boxed tea; (6) In order to invite the Ministry of Industry to treat foreign-owned tea businesses from the perspective of self-control, advocate the principle of official supervision and merchant management, and provide assistance to promote progress; (7) For domestic exported tea, the government should determine the policy of official supervision and merchant management, and urgently improve it; (8) Please allow the Anhui Provincial Government to consider the difficulties of merchants and allow foreign-owned tea businesses to resume black tea operations to solve their problems and observe the initial effect; (9) Find ways to avoid transporting boxed tea by car; (10) Request the government to carefully study and earnestly discuss the control of foreign-owned boxed tea; (11) Request the government to exempt Wenzhou raw tea from taxes; (D) Other Group: (1) Improve tea box production; (2) Reduce the number of triangular wooden strips in tea boxes and slightly increase the thickness of tea box boards; (3) Foreign-owned tea boxes should be reformed urgently; (4) Unify tea names; (5) Request the government to implement the exemption of tea transit tax; (6) Unify the scale for tea; (7) Verify operating capital and issue business licenses to show uniformity and caution; (8) Promote tea by using advertising and propaganda; (9) Please ask the government to abolish the prohibition of drinking tea in the Shanghai New Transportation Branch; (10) Hold tea exhibitions and competitions; (11) Suggest that the government pay attention to foreign propaganda in China; (12) Collect propaganda fees based on the selling price of tea; (13) Suggest that the government cultivate tea talents at all levels; (14) Organize joint offices in various improvement sites; (15) Solicit ancient tea drinking utensils and tea documents.

Situation Eases, River Cargo Crowded for Loading: Hunan Water Shallow, Navigation Route Cut Off, Freight Rates Soar by 60% 122

In the past two weeks, Shanghai's Yangtze River shipping companies temporarily suspended loading of all cargo destined for Jiujiang, Hankou, and Hunan Province due to the serious situation. Goods were stockpiled in Shanghai warehouses. Moreover, due to shallow water in Hunan, transportation was difficult, causing warehouses to be even more crowded. Now that the situation has gradually eased, the Yangtze River shipping companies are taking advantage of this opportunity to rush to load and export the previously stockpiled goods, starting yesterday. Cotton yarn, cloth, white sugar, salt, and daily necessities are the main commodities. They are being reported to China Merchants, Sanbei, NingShao, Taikoo, and Jardine Matheson companies for transportation to Xun and Han ports. Yesterday, the Jianghua ship loaded more than 30,000 dan of cargo. Other Yangtze River transport ships were also fully loaded, and even more could not be cleared through customs in time for loading, which will be continued today and tomorrow. In total, the accumulated goods to be transported to the Yangtze River are worth at least 7 million yuan. Sanbei Company has specially added the Xingshi transport ship, and the China Merchants Bureau also plans to add two ships to operate, because there is still a huge amount of cargo waiting to be transported. The Xiang River is shallow, has receded to 3.2 feet, and the navigation route is blocked, only reaching Dulin Tan. Shanghai's outgoing cargo is also crowded, and the six companies, in order to maintain Hunan's transportation and avoid interruption, have hired a large number of civilian boats at Lulin Tan to transship goods. The shallow water fee for Changsha has already increased by 10%, and it has been decided to increase it by another 40%. The shallow water fee from Shanghai to Changde will increase by 60%.
