Miscellaneous Talk

The Third Landlord and the Fourth Tenant 191

— Jiang Gong

—— One of Shanghai's Special Products

Shanghai is a place where every inch of land is worth gold. The high land prices and exorbitant rents are astonishing. The prevalence of the second landlord system further forces ordinary residents to waste more money on rent, yet they cannot find a reasonably satisfactory place to live, increasing their complaints and grievances. However, those who become third tenants are trapped by economic hardship and have no choice but to drink poison to quench their thirst, keeping their eyes wide open as they endure the abuse of the second landlord!

In the inland areas, poor small citizens or impoverished households who cannot afford to rent an entire house on their own, there are also many families who live together within a large gate. In Beijing, this is called a "big courtyard." Living here is limited to extremely destitute small families. Those who consider themselves middle or upper class, no matter how poor they may be, would rather die than stoop down and mix with them, fearing that it would diminish their noble personality and tarnish their clean reputation. But these are all directly rented out by the main landlord. Occasionally, a tenant, because there are more houses than people, wants to save expenses and sublets the remaining rooms to others. This is not unheard of, but it accounts for only a very small number. As for using this to make a profit, relying on it as a way to make money and support oneself, or even not living there themselves, but specifically renting several rooms to store merchandise or personal property, that only exists in Shanghai's so-called second landlord system.

Shanghai's society is inherently a deformed organization, and its contents are so dark that it is horrifying. Therefore, it easily generates many special classes and performs countless ghostly tricks. The second landlord is one of these special classes. I often say that the main reason why most residents of Shanghai experience hardship and economic pressure is not due to the high cost of living, but because of those vermin parasitic on the dark side of this society, who layer upon layer exploit the masses. Thus, the poor become poorer, the suffering suffer more, while they do not till the land or weave clothes, but rely on cleverly sucking the fat from the poor. One by one, they become fat-headed and big-bellied, looking quite good.

The second landlord's only occupation is to take advantage of the high cost of rent and the weak economic capacity of most citizens. They advance a sum of money to rent a number of houses, and then sublet them room by room at even more exorbitant prices, acting as intermediaries who manipulate the market, sitting back and reaping the benefits. With a mere turn of the hand, they can not only live rent-free but also solve their living problems. In the heyday of the French Concession a few years ago, houses in the Baoyu Li and Baoxing Li areas were particularly expensive due to their central location and high demand, with each wing room renting for around a hundred yuan. Yet, those who came to rent were still fighting over them, and some were even willing to pay extra fees to become second landlords. At that time, as long as you rented a three-story house, you could easily earn several hundred yuan a month. Can you find such a good business anywhere else but Shanghai? Furthermore, if there were any natural disasters or man-made calamities in other places, such as the Qi-Lu War or the great flood in Hankou, people with some resources would flee to Shanghai to take refuge. That would be another good opportunity for them to hoard goods and extort high prices. (Many economic experts specifically found excuses to ask the original third tenants to move out, and then reposted rental notices, with the whole family sleeping on the floor under the stairs, freeing up the rooms to rent to refugees, hoping to make a big fortune during this period.) The main landlord who owns the property cannot share this right. In the past two years, Shanghai has also been surrounded by a recession. The market is sluggish, credit is tight, and even Nanjing Road, the most prosperous commercial street, has many vacant rooms. Shops sealed with "ten" signs for rent arrears and defaults are everywhere. The call for rent reduction is rising to the clouds. At this time, the second landlords may secretly worry about the shaking of their position, and of course, the profits they receive are not what they used to be. However, in any case, they will not do business at a loss! (However, recently, there are many who post empty room signs, and many third tenants who cannot pay the rent. If the skin does not exist, what will the hair attach to? Therefore, under today's circumstances, the second landlord can be both possible and impossible!)

In the past, the second landlords were mostly parasites who squeezed the marrow and sweat of the third tenants. Most residents suffered increased burdens because of them, living in even more expensive houses. They demanded rent more fiercely than the main landlord. At the main landlord's place, you could still owe rent for three months, but the second landlord would not allow a day's delay. That cold, icy, and impartially ruthless expression was even uglier than that of Yama Bao. Therefore, they often had conflicts with the third tenants, almost like enemies, rarely living in peace. Furthermore, the brightness of the electric light and the duration of the night light became the focus of disputes between the two sides. (Of course, there are also many second landlords with noble behavior who do not aim to make a profit. When subletting the remaining rooms, they are unwilling to easily rent them out to other than upstanding tenants. But these are ultimately fewer than those who hoard and profit, especially hard to find in the slums!)

The most ridiculous thing is that there is also a kind of third landlord. He is originally a third tenant, renting a large room or two from the second landlord. If he encounters someone willing to pay a higher rent, he sees that there is profit to be made and sublets half of it to someone else. Generally, he also posts a "Available Room for Rent" sign, finally getting to experience being a landlord, finally becoming a member of the bourgeoisie. Because there are third landlords, there are also so-called fourth tenants. These people are naturally a little better off than those whose mansions are set up in straw sheds!

The Phoenixes Replace the Nest 192

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Brotherly Affection Hides Letter, Pities Weak Sister; Noble Air of Poetry and Books Peeks at Shadow, Laughs at Poor Scholar

It was summer, and the slopes around the small nunnery were covered with green grass, an inch long, like a green carpet spread on the ground. Although there were few trees, the fences of the vegetable gardens were covered with green vines. Inside the short walls of the vegetable garden, rows of sunflower stalks and piles of melon trellises added some interest. The Stone Guanyin Nunnery, under a few sparse trees, revealed a stretch of red walls. In the faint morning light, the early morning bell rang a few clear times. Looking out from here, one felt a sense of emptiness in one's heart. Wuxuan and his sister, stepping on the dewdrops on the grass slopes, walked in silence, not mentioning anything important to each other. Menglan stopped at the crossroads and asked, "Brother, are we going to the Reading Platform?" Wuxuan laughed, "It's cool in the morning, why should we go up and down, working up a sweat? There are two clean stones on that Tiger Stone. We can go sit there. I probably have a few things to talk to you about." Menglan hesitated. Although she couldn't figure out what he meant, she didn't dare to refuse and simply followed him. Climbing a few layers of earthen slopes, they reached a flat, rocky area. In the cracks between the broken stones, clusters of short grass grew outwards. The dewdrops on the grass heads were still hanging there, clear and bright, indicating that the night air had not completely dissipated. As a result, when they reached this place, the morning breeze blowing on their bodies was still a bit cool. There wasn't a soul in sight, only birds flying in the sky. Wuxuan stopped and looked at Menglan, saying solemnly, "I didn't bring you here to play. I have something to give you." As he spoke, he reached into his pocket and fumbled for a while, taking out Zhang Guoqi's letter. When Menglan saw the letter, a flush of red immediately spread across her face. Moreover, the letter was already opened. The situation didn't need to be explained in detail. Her heart was pounding like a startled deer, thumping from the inside out. Wuxuan handed the letter directly to her, and she had no choice but to take it. However, her head was already lowered and she couldn't lift it up. (84)

Finance: Standard Gold Futures Plummets Another 3.4 Yuan; Standard Below Maintained… Weakness Turns Wavering 193

The gold market yesterday saw pure gold decline with heavier selling pressure, retreating below the reference price. However, after the low, there were obvious buying interests, turning to consolidation after weakness, ultimately wavering. Early morning saw overseas silver markets reacting to the English contraction and the American stability. Monterri futures silver prices contracted by 0.5 to 1.5 basis points. Exchange rates rose across the board. London raw gold fell by 4.5 pence. The Central Bank's official rate announcement revealed English and American rates both stable. Customs gold unit contracted by 6%. The standard futures gold price announcement fell to 1153.7 yuan. Off-market preliminary trading opened with bids at 56 yuan, but Dadecheng, Yuanmaoyong all sold off, retreating to 4 yuan. Chunyuan Yongxian's buying managed to provide some support. The morning opened lower. After the opening, large players continued to close out, gradually declining. Although there were struggles midway, the market price was still slight. The HSBC bank's official rate announcement revealed English and American rates both stable, and it was still difficult to stimulate the market. Later, although the silver balancing tax contracted by 0.5%, buyers were active on the dip, and slightly recovered. After entering, supply and demand both declined and turned to consolidation. The afternoon market opened peacefully, with limited fluctuation. Afterward, as sellers watched, demand slightly surged and gradually rose, but many continued to unload, ultimately unable to escape consolidation. A record of the day's market conditions follows:

The morning opened at 1154.2 yuan, 2 yuan lower than before National Day. Dingkang, Hongli, Hengyu, Yuanmaoyong all sold off from 4.3 yuan, declining to 2.8 yuan. Dadecheng, Yuanmaoyong, Dingkang maintained on the dip, rising to 3.2 yuan. Qingfa, Yongyuan, Yuanmaoyong, Dadecheng soon sold off again. The HSBC bank's official rate announcement revealed English and American rates both stable, and fell to 2.3 yuan. Qiafeng, Yongcheng, Dayu, Xinxiang, Dingkang took in strips on the dip. Although the silver balancing tax was small, only 0.5%, it still recovered to 3 yuan. Yuanmaoyong, Dadecheng supplied on the high, retreating to 2.5 yuan. Futai Henglai Jin. The noon close was 1152.7 yuan.

Yuxinxiang, Yongde, Daheng, Shen, Da Yongxiang, Fengcheng, Da Qiafeng, Yong all bought, gradually rising to 3.6 yuan. Yuanmaoyong supplied on the high, falling back to 2.9 yuan. Chengda, Qiafengyong still took in, rising to 3.3 yuan. The close was 1153.1 yuan. Flat after the close.

The settlement price, according to the Central Bank's standard futures gold price, was announced to have declined to 1153.7 yuan, approximately 6 yuan lower according to the closing price. The current month's booked price was 1148 yuan. November's was 1153 yuan. The morning water supplement was 1148 yuan. Red gold's price was stable at 1162.2 yuan. Tianjin goods were quoted at an additional 14 yuan. Cooked red gold's buying price was 12 yuan, with no counterparty. The selling price was quoted at an additional 17.5 yuan. Shengyuan, Yongtongfeng Heng sold over 300 taels, absorbed by domestic banks and gold shops.

Trading inside the market was not heavy. In summary, Qiafengyong, Yuxinxiang, Chengda, Daheng, Dingkang, Shunmao, Dachangxiang, Wanxing, Tongfeng, Heng etc. were on the buying side. Hengyu, Chunyuan, Yongfuxing, Yongfuyu, Shen, Da Yong, Qingfa, Yong Jinfengyong, Qianyuanchangyong etc. were on the selling side. Dingkang Yuanmaoyong Dadecheng advanced and then retreated.

Checking the day's market conditions, it was weak. The morning opened at 1154.2 yuan, the close was 1153.1 yuan. The highest price was 1154.3 yuan, the lowest price was 1152.3 yuan, with a fluctuation of 2 yuan. The remaining current month's strips were 490. In total, there were 8 bullish companies, 6 bearish companies. Yesterday, the Hua Merchants Securities Exchange initially rose due to the easing of Sino-Japanese issues, then fell due to rumors of a political disturbance in a certain country, and ultimately turned tight again due to bearish covering. Number 11 continued selling, and the market price suddenly rose by 0.2 to 0.55 yuan. The second session saw selling of numbers 10 and 11, buying of numbers 5 and 6, and a need for number 4. Yarn & Cotton: Yarn Sales Exceed 5,000 Bales; Futures Yarn Bearish Covering; Warehouse Stock Decreasing Daily; Near-Term Soars, New Peak Appears; Far-Term Slower, Inversion More Obvious 196

The yarn market is trending firm, with a rampant rising trend. Because existing yarn sales are developing, customers are coming in droves. Factories report a complete lack of existing goods. The stock in the exchange's warehouses is decreasing daily. Selling prices are flying higher and higher, exceeding the standard yarn price by a margin of 5.6 yuan. Therefore, the bearish side is active, and covering is urgently needed. It is said that the amount of yarn in the warehouses has decreased to 12,000-13,000 bales.

The futures yarn market is enthusiastic.

The futures yarn market opened in the morning, with all months rising uniformly. Because yarn sales prices are strong, and existing goods are extremely scarce, each group is particularly eager to buy yarn in the warehouses. Therefore, market sentiment is enthusiastic, and buying pressure is quite strong. October's rose every session, and discovered new peaks after September 29th, reaching 212.1 yuan. The close saw the far-term rising trend slightly moderate. Dafeng, Mingde, Changyu, Wang Taixing, Taichang, Changfeng, Shengyuan, Xincheng etc. uniformly sold off. New Family and Hygiene

— Edited by Dr. Shen Zhaoquan

Futures Lower Than Spot Prices, Cotton Market Decline Difficult 198

The cotton market is calm, but the US and Indian cotton markets are softening. Large players are using coarse cotton to pressure the market this month, and sources from various regions are gradually increasing. Therefore, the cotton market is not as expensive as the yarn market. However, the price of Futures Cotton is several yuan lower than spot cotton, so a decline is practically difficult.

Futures Cotton Rises After a Fall 199

The futures cotton market opened with declines due to weakness in US cotton. Trading was suspended for two days, resulting in overall drops. Market sentiment was ordinary, and most speculators were buying yarn and selling cotton. Furthermore, large players were using coarse Russian cotton to exert pressure in the near months, leading to a softer cotton market. Prices for all months fell slightly by a dime. In the second session, yarn sales were reported to be active, factories had constant demand, and prices in various producing areas were not loosening. The third session jumped up by twenty or thirty cents, and closing was flat. Da Fu, Yu Da, Zhen Da, Shen Ji, Wang Tai Xing, and Yuan Yi continued to sell. However, Heng Xing, Ming De, Guang Shuang, Yu Chang, Yuan Yi, Sheng Yuan, Yu Kang, and Tong He and other buyers bought. The result of futures cotton trading was that prices for all months rose by five cents to two dimes compared to the previous day's closing price. The afternoon session opened with a lively yarn market and high demand for spot cotton from factories, which led short sellers to cover their positions and pushed the market upward. As a result, prices for all months rose by another five cents to one and a half dimes compared to the morning closing price. Sales included: Da Fu: 4,500 dan, Yu Da: 4,500 dan, Zhen Da: 1,500 dan, Tong He: 1,600 dan, Chang He: 1,500 dan, Shen Ji: 5,300 dan, Wang Tai Xing: 2,100 dan, Yuan Yu Yuan: 2,100 dan, Shen Chang: 1,600 dan, Da Chang Cheng: 1,800 dan, Run Kang: 4,500 dan, He Yu: 1,500 dan, Mao Jin Guang Feng: 6,000 zu, Ju Yu: 1,400 dan, Ming De: 1,800 dan, Xing Chang: 2,700 dan, Yuan Yi Er Er: 2,700 dan, Sheng Yuan: 2,900 dan, Fu Kang: 1,900 dan, Xin Chang: 1,800 dan, Da Hui: 1,900 dan, Chang Yu: 2,000 dan, Ren Feng: 5,300 dan. The high and low prices for the day are listed on the left.

Constant Spot Cotton Demand

Spot cotton consumption is still reasonably good, and factory demand continues unabated. Sources include 2,280 bales of Yao cotton and Tong cotton.

Bombay Cotton Industry Weekly Report 200

Market conditions were slightly softer last week, with profit-taking by long positions being the primary reason. At the same time, spot prices were weak due to a large increase in inventory. Export news was moderate, with Japan continuing to purchase. Attention was paid to Karachi cotton for import. The mainland market was sluggish. In the Netherlands, transactions were reportedly brisk. Cotton harvest conditions were generally satisfactory, but there was a slight lack of rain. The statistics for the past week are appended below (unit: thousands of cantons):

Yarn, Cotton, and Cloth Prices All Decline 201

Osaka, December 12th dispatch: Futures yarn fell by one dime to one yuan, with the near month at 213.2 yuan and the distant month at 204.4 yuan. Futures cotton fell by three to five dimes, with the near month at 66.6 yuan and the distant month at 65.2 yuan.

Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth Market Prices Continue to Rise 203

As soon as the futures yarn market opened yesterday, spot prices rose, and sluggish yarn sales greatly improved, causing the interdependent cloth market to also soar. After several trading sessions in a day, the result was that compared to last week, white cotton fine cloth and fine twill spot prices rose (per bolt) by one dime, light-weight coarse twill rose (per bolt) by one and a half dimes, heavy-weight rose (per bolt) by more than three dimes, light-weight coarse cloth rose by five cents, and heavy-weight coarse cloth rose by twenty or thirty cents. The prices of finished dyed and printed cloths also rose, by two and a half to three dimes per bolt. Shipments to various ports, especially to the upper reaches of the Sichuan, Guangdong, and Yangtze rivers, were most active. The shortage of various goods is intensifying daily. Even though adding to transactions is still extremely crowded, and market prices are rising sharply, buyers' enthusiasm is not dampened. At the same time, because raw materials such as yarn are so popular, factories are also experiencing fears of raw material shortages, so they have repeatedly raised factory prices. Factory-produced Dong goods, fine cloth, and fine twill, especially the blue cloth and colored twill produced by dyeing factories recently, are selling slowly, so demand is not urgent, and the price increases are also slightly moderate. However, this factory's fine twill and fine cloth are being eagerly sought after by merchants looking for spot goods, so sales are exceptionally strong.

Camel Down Factory Rushing to Produce Winter-Selling Goods, Supply Cannot Keep Up 204

Wide and narrow striped, plain-colored camel down is currently selling briskly. Most merchants completed their purchases last month, but those at Weiyi Street are still adding to their orders. Most of the existing stock in the factories has been sold out, so they are now working day and night to rush production, which is quite busy. Those priced around one yuan are selling the fastest. The factory's production is feared to be unable to keep up. In total, in the past few days, transactions of the striped and plain-colored fine and wide camel down have averaged over 5,000 yards per day. We Lun Tiger picture is sold for 2.25 yuan, Tian Xiang Invincible fleece back is sold for 2.45 yuan, Wei Feng Golden Lion is sold for 1 yuan, Zhang Hua Cotton Mou is sold for 1.05 yuan, Jing Lun Moon Rabbit is sold for 1.575 yuan.

Sugar Market: Sugar Prices Rarely Fluctuate 205

The sugar market was stable yesterday. The association quoted prices for grades such as No. 24 coarse granulated white, Dong White, and native fine white at original prices. In the Hao market, a Chao merchant offered 86 bags of Zhuang red at 14.8 yuan, and 49 bags of Huanggang Qing at 14 yuan. A Jian merchant, Da Lai, offered over 300 bags of Zhang Diao Qing, with the higher prices at 13.5 yuan, then 13 yuan to 12.8 yuan.

The Joint Company held its first tender this week for Fan-Yue sugar, with a total quota of 9,968 bags. The price remained unchanged. The sales included 275 bags of Shunde Wu Yang coarse white at 21.5 yuan, ten bags of Xinshi sugar at 20.3 yuan, and one thousand bags of Qu Xi Factory sugar at 21.2 yuan. There were no sales.

North-South Goods: Quanzhou Pao Yuan Drops Sharply, Then Rises Slightly 206

The price of Quanzhou Pao Yuan has been in a standoff for ten days because the traders and merchants have not been able to agree on a price. Yesterday, they finally came closer to an agreement. Large-size goods fell by 3-4 yuan due to oversupply, while medium-grade goods fell by about 1 yuan. Small-size goods rose slightly by several dimes due to a shortage of goods. A total of over 6,000 boxes were offered, and the market was stable.

Grain: Northern Merchants Hoarding Flour, Buying Enthusiasm Unstoppable, Record Highs Not Seen in Recent Years 207

After the market opened yesterday morning, the flour market once again showed a sharp rise across all months. Because the market was closed for two days, quotations for foreign wheat from both Chicago and Canada generally rose by about one yuan. Domestically, due to the Sino-Japanese issue, northern grain merchants were united, leading to rising quotations. In Shanghai, people were excited because they saw rising prices abroad and active sales. The opening price jumped by forty or fifty cents, and then rose by another dime as buying interest remained strong. By the time the afternoon session opened, the situation had become more serious. The highest price for the current month reached 3.495 yuan, and the November price also jumped over the 5-yuan mark to 5.175 yuan. The longest-dated month, such as March, even reached 3.64 yuan. These market conditions are the highest new records in the past four or five years. However, after the third session, rumors of the dissolution of a domestic cabinet caused sentiment to soften slightly, and prices fell back by twenty or thirty cents from the highest levels, but were still significantly higher by thirty, forty, or fifty cents compared to before the market closed.

Both Futures and Spot Wheat See Rising Prices -- Flour Sales to the North are Brisk… Concerns that Supplies May Run Out -- 208

The futures wheat market rose across all months yesterday morning because foreign wheat prices had risen by about one yuan in the past two days. On the flour sales side, the opening was due to brisk purchases from the North, with inventories already not very high, and future sources of wheat becoming increasingly scarce. All of this has deeply affected the market, so there were no unexpected surges and things remained calm. Otherwise, it would have been difficult to suppress the momentum. Therefore, after opening, prices for each month rose by six, seven, or eight cents. Later, as opinions between buyers and sellers approached, prices stabilized. When the afternoon session opened, prices initially rose again, continuing to be better by three to five cents compared to the morning, and transactions were brisk. Later, as the flour market turned flat, sentiment softened slightly, and the results were generally similar to the morning. The spot wheat market also saw prices rise by five cents because the market price was so high that factories were collectively holding back from buying, so things remained peaceful. Shandong Zizhou wheat was heard to be 5.5 yuan, Yanghe wheat was 5.45 yuan, secondary 5.4 yuan, Bengbu wheat was 5.47 yuan, secondary 5.42 yuan, Jiangbei wheat was 5.28 yuan, secondary 5.25 yuan, Gaoyou wheat was 5.45 yuan, secondary 5.4 yuan, Zhuzhen wheat was 5.35 yuan, and Nanjing Kanming wheat was 5.1 yuan. Fu Xin purchased 15,000 bags, and Shen Da purchased 2,000 bags.

River Rice Price Plunge Stimulates Sales 209

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, sources from various gangs were still abundant, with a total of 54 or 55 boats arriving, carrying a total of 1,300 or 1,400 shi. However, sales in this street were scarce. Only the Bao Wei, Qing Yan, Dalian, and other gangs purchased nearly 1,000 bags of Yaozhong Baige and over 300 bags of Bo Po. The Wen Tianjin Gang purchased 1,500 bags of Hou Xin Geng. Therefore, market conditions were difficult to maintain and continued to be weak. Yaozhong Baige prices fell by one or two dimes, and Hou Xin Geng plummeted by half a yuan. Du Yang and other varieties of Xin Jian also fell by one or two dimes, and Bo Po Geng also depreciated by one or two dimes. Only Xin Yin Yuan, because the arrival of goods was not large, remained unchanged. However, observing the afternoon market situation, sentiment seemed to be active after the sharp decline. If the source of goods is not strong, there may be a temporary hope of stability.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 43 or 44 boats arrived from various routes in the river. Sales of various goods in the market were slightly active for Po Geng and Xin Geng, and the remaining goods were flat. The market situation was that high-grade Po Geng rose slightly by a dime, while medium- and lower-grade fell by one or two dimes. Xin Geng continued to fall by two, three, or four dimes. Xin Yang, Du Jian, Xin Chen, and Bian Yuan followed with declines of one or two dimes. Yao Zhong, Bu Jian, and Ke Jian prices did not fluctuate much.

Guangdong Merchants Briskly Purchase Brown and Milled Rice 210

Yesterday, the Ke Xian rice market was quite active. Because trading on the National Day and Sunday was slow, both the North and South gangs went to the market to buy rice yesterday. Although arrivals have been brisk for several days and inventories are also sufficient, the market was lively and strong. Guangdong merchants had the best sales. In addition to brown rice, milled rice from various routes was also purchased in whole batches. Northern merchants also had strong demand. Shantou merchants also continued to inquire. It is estimated that 6,600 bags of Jiangxi rice, 5,300 bags of Xiang rice, 300 bags of Taiwanese Xian rice, 200 bags of Han Xi rice, and 1,000 bags of Jiaxing Zao Jian were sold throughout the day.

The Issue of Blood Transfusions 221

— Song Guobin

Recently, a certain hospital in Shanghai organized a blood transfusion team to handle blood purchase matters, which has attracted social attention. A certain lawyer once submitted a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration to interpret whether this matter constitutes a crime. The reasons he holds are summarized as follows:

(1) Blood is an essential element of life. The person from whom blood is drawn risks death from blood loss, while the patient themselves gains no real benefit.

(2) Although the blood donation is voluntary on the part of the injured person, voluntarily injuring oneself is no different from suicide. If instigating or helping another person commit suicide is a crime, then instigating and helping another person injure themselves should also be a crime.

(3) Drawing the blood of the poor to benefit the rich, making the rich stronger and the poor weaker, and the rich live while the poor die, is truly intolerable by the law.

Regarding the lawyer's suggestion, we believe that the first and second points are open to discussion. Blood transfusion is one of the scientific therapies and holds a significant position in medicine. In terms of its effectiveness, it can indeed bring the dying back to life. The lawyer's statement that it offers "no real benefit" is simply unfounded. As for the donor, because the amount drawn is not excessive, the loss suffered is also limited. With a little rest, they can recover. It will definitely not lead to "death from blood loss" as the lawyer said. Blood transfusion therapy is a method of supplementing the deficient with the surplus. It certainly has its value.

The second point raised by the lawyer is the issue of injury. He believes that although the person from whom blood is drawn voluntarily injures themselves, the practitioner is guilty of instigating or helping another person voluntarily injure themselves. In my opinion, this reason is difficult to establish. Regardless of whether the phrase "instigating and helping another person voluntarily injure themselves" is explicitly stated in the law, even if it is considered to fully align with the principles of legislation, the law clearly states that "justifiable acts are not punishable." This can be interpreted as professionals exercising the rights that fall within their professional scope. A doctor, by virtue of their profession, has the right to use anesthetics and perform amputations within the scope of medicine at any time. Because this is a justifiable act, it cannot be considered injury. Blood transfusion is a scientific therapy and is, of course, a justifiable act. Moreover, the blood donation is voluntary and not instigated by the doctor. Furthermore, the donor can recover with a little rest after the blood donation, and there is no great danger. There is even less reason to speak of injury!

The third point raised by the lawyer has some valid reasons. Drawing the blood of the poor to benefit the rich is, in any case, inhumane. If the doctor profits from this, collecting blood at extremely low prices and transfusing it to others at the highest price, earning a significant profit in the process, this behavior is worse than that of human traffickers and greedy officials who exploit the people.

The lawyer's suggestions have been stated above. Now, I will briefly state my suggestions regarding this issue:

(1) The Human Issue: Although blood transfusion is not a criminal act, buying and selling blood and drawing the blood of the poor to inject into the rich is indeed the most inhumane thing. It must be understood that the fundamental condition of this issue is that the donor is not induced by money but is entirely motivated by compassion. Among humans, those most full of compassion are religious figures! Chinese monks and nuns, and foreign male and female clergy, are all compassionate and willing to sacrifice themselves to save the world. Let us look at their religious leaders, the Buddha who fed himself to a tiger, and Jesus who was nailed to the cross. Their great spirit of sacrifice is truly worthy of emulation by religious people. Therefore, I hope that the religious people of the world, based on compassion, will automatically unite to organize a blood transfusion organization to provide blood to anemic patients. The ancients said, "Cutting one's arm to heal a parent" is driven by filial piety. Transfusing blood to save people is driven by compassion. Moreover, most religions advocate celibacy, free from the disturbances of desire, and their blood is even cleaner. Religious people of the world! Instead of chanting scriptures, worshiping Buddha, or praying to God, why not each donate a drop of blood to do this good deed that is truly beneficial to humanity?

(2) The Use of Blood Transfusions: Blood transfusions are even more important during wartime. When war begins, those soldiers who fight for the country and the nation shed their own blood in large quantities to win glory for the country and the nation. They are injured! They bleed! Doctors use surgical clamps to stop their blood vessels and stop the bleeding, but some eventually lose their lives due to excessive blood loss. At this time, how should the people in the rear do their best to supply these wounded heroes? Material supply is certainly important, but is it not more valuable to use their own blood to supply them, voluntarily sending it to doctors for extraction, so that these bleeding soldiers can receive blood supplementation and easily recover their health, returning to the battlefield to kill the enemy? Soldiers who kill the enemy on the front lines are directly shedding blood, while those in the rear who transfuse blood are indirectly shedding blood. Both are national heroes and have contributed to the country.

In short, blood transfusion itself is neither good nor evil. It is the motive and the object that determines good and evil. The motive should not be money, and the object should not be class. Instead, the motive should be compassion and loyalty, and the object should be humanity and the country.

(B) Relief Center Clinic

(XIII) Medical Conditions

(A) Hospitals

On Rickettsia and Rickettsial Diseases (3) 223

— Chen Duanbai

(III) Bacteriological Aspects

Although the biological classification of Rickettsia is not yet very clear, the fact that it belongs to the bacteria family, or something similar to bacteria, (Schizomyceten, commonly known as bacteria) can be determined based on its reproductive method (constriction and transverse division). However, it is difficult to find it living inside cells (Cytotrop) in the blood of patients and animals. Conversely, it is easy to demonstrate in the digestive tract of vectors and animal tissues, such as the testicles and Descemet's membrane cells, (Descemet Membran & Hodenzellen) during a considerable period. This is one of the distinctive features of Rickettsia. It cannot be successfully cultured using ordinary or special media. Only tissue culture can be used, Gewebeskultur Tissue Culture. This is the second distinctive feature of Rickettsia. Its size is generally 0.3 to 0.5 U, 0.3-0.5粁 (thousandth of a mm). Among all known bacteria, none is smaller than it. This is the third distinctive feature of Rickettsia. Rickettsia is non-filterable. It cannot pass through the Berkeleld & Chamberland filter. Its body is spherical, slightly elliptical, and consistently arranged in streptococcus-like shapes, with transverse bands in the middle to connect them. Among the various pigment sensitivities, Giemsa staining is the most suitable. After staining, it appears deep purple, spherical or rod-shaped, with the transverse band appearing light blue. The outlines of each Rickettsia are rarely clear. During the degeneration period of Rickettsia, its ability to receive pigments also decreases, often being blurred and light, making it difficult to distinguish from cell granules. When Rickettsia proliferates, it can be in the form of thin filaments or staphylococcus-like clusters. Its ability to proliferate in the human body is not as strong as its proliferation in arthropods and other animals such as rabbits. The fact that it proliferates outside cells has not yet been confirmed. Animal inoculation is most convenient with rabbit testicles and the anterior chamber of the eye. For clinical research, the Macacus Fascafus Japanese monkey is the most suitable.

(IV) Types and Geographic Distribution of Rickettsial Diseases

As far as we know now, there are various rickettsial diseases:

(1) Typhus Fever (Flecktypbus)

(2) Trench Fever (Febris Wolhynica)

(3) Rocky Mountain Spotted Fever

(4) Tsutsugamushi Fever (Tautsugamusi Fieber)

Others such as Tabardillo, Brill Disease, Mauchu TyplivsGndiwisch Flloklieber, Mexican typhus fever, and Manchurian typhus fever, as well as endemic typhus fever, are all friends in the typhus fever family.

In terms of its geographic area, countries in Southeastern Europe, such as Romania, Czechoslovakia, Poland, and the border between Poland and Russia, North America, Eastern Asia, Southern China, and Japan, Taiwan, and the South Sea Islands all have traces of Rickettsia. The history of its development certainly goes back more than twenty years, it's just that its details were not known before and it was confused with other suspected diseases.

(V) Pathological Aspects

When Rickettsia invades the human body, the first step is the skin. The changes it causes are perivascular infiltration, especially in the capillaries Perirasuclare Infiltration. Lymphatic vessels are also equally affected. As the situation progresses, this change can reach the subcutaneous tissue. Japanese Tsutsugamushi disease researcher and pathologist Rin Kawamura also studied the cortical pathology and biological changes of Tsutsugamushi disease Rickettsia. According to him, Rickettsia grows in mononuclear cells Histiocyt from the third to the eighth or ninth day after infection, which is the proliferation period. After reaching its peak, it gradually degenerates and decreases. After the ninth day, its morphology is incomplete within two or three days, its number is greatly reduced, and it eventually disappears completely. When studying skin allergic reactions (Tsutsugamushi disease), as a necessary stage of the preliminary work, the author also conducted an experiment. The results were completely consistent with Kawamura's report. The pathological tissue changes caused by Rickettsia reproduction are (1) perivascular inflammation, (2) infiltration, (3) degeneration, and (4) necrosis. The blood vessels undergo extreme dilation, and the phenomenon caused by this is, of course, the slowing of blood flow and the exudation of blood due to the weakening of the blood vessel walls. The changes in the skin throughout are only two weeks. The recovery situation is the reduction of infiltration, the contraction of blood vessels, and a gradual return to the pre-disease state, without leaving any scars. The pathological changes caused by Rickettsia in other organs are nothing more than perivascular inflammation and the associated or subsequent phenomena.

Common Knowledge Q&A about Diseases 224

— Cheng Hanzhang

(93) Acute Gastric Mucositis (Gastritis Acuta)

(Q) What is acute gastric mucositis?

(A) This is one of the most common diseases of the stomach, which is an acute inflammation of the gastric mucosa. Doctors commonly call it acute gastric catarrh.

(Q) What is the main cause of this disease?

(A) The main causes of acute gastric mucositis are overeating, indiscriminately eating food that is too cold or too hot or spoiled, and not chewing food sufficiently when eating.

(Q) Besides these causes, what else can cause acute inflammation of the gastric mucosa?

(A) Accidentally swallowing corrosive substances such as acids, alkalis, carbolic acid, mercuric chloride, phosphorus, and arsenic can also cause acute gastric mucositis. Also, people with acute febrile diseases, anemia, and weakness often develop this disease concurrently.

(Q) What digestive symptoms do patients with acute gastric mucositis experience?

(A) The main symptoms are indigestion, which includes loss of appetite, pressure in the stomach, aversion to eating, thirst, nausea, vomiting, noisy stomach, and belching.

(Q) What symptoms appear in the patient's mouth?

(A) A thick coating on the tongue, a sticky taste, bad breath, and herpes labialis.

(Q) What are the abnormalities in the stool and urine?

(A) The stool tends to be constipated, and the amount of urine is less than usual.

(Q) Does the patient's body have a fever?

(A) There is usually a moderate fever, around 38 degrees Celsius.

(Q) Are gastric function and secretion affected?

(A) After suffering from acute gastric mucositis, gastric function naturally declines, secretion also decreases, and the amount of free hydrochloric acid also decreases.

(Q) How is acute gastric mucositis diagnosed?

(A) If the patient has a fever, it can easily be confused with typhoid fever. It should be differentiated by the presence or absence of splenomegaly and rose spots.

(Q) What is the treatment for acute gastric mucositis?

(A) The first thing is to remove the accumulated contents in the stomach, which is to make the patient vomit or perform gastric lavage; if that is not possible, then inject "apomorphine" to induce vomiting. If it is too late, and it is suspected that it has reached the intestines, then a laxative should be administered.

(Q) What kind of food should the patient eat?

(A) First, abstain from food for one or two days, only drinking things like malt soup and kudzu root soup. Afterwards, eat some rice porridge, fish, eggs, meat juice, and potatoes in small amounts, gradually moving on to ordinary food.

(Q) What should be done about stomach pain and vomiting?

(A) At this time, warmth can be applied to the upper abdomen, or an anesthetic can be taken internally. When thirsty, drink some soda or cold drinks.

(Q) When the illness has recovered, how should medicine be used?

(A) During the recovery period, a stomachic can be administered to stimulate appetite.

Hygiene Tips for Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Diseases 225

— Tang Renjin

(103) Otitic Meningitis

There are many types of meningitis. What people generally refer to as meningitis is epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis. It is incorrect to assume that meningitis only refers to this one type. According to the different types of meningitis, besides epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis, there are also tuberculous meningitis, serous meningitis, and many other distinctions. These fall under the scope of internal medicine and will not be discussed here. What I want to talk about now is otitic meningitis.

The occurrence of otitic meningitis generally cannot escape three pathways: First, it originates from otitis media or mastoiditis. Second, it originates from otitis media combined with suppurative labyrinthitis. Third, it originates from inner ear inflammation and other complications. Because the cause originates in the ear, it is called otitic meningitis. Otitic meningitis generally occurs more frequently in children. If it is caused by chronic otitis media, children around ten years old are most susceptible. It is rarely seen in adults. However, the bone of the mastoid process in young children is very thin, so when young children develop mastoiditis, one must be careful to prevent the occurrence of otitic meningitis.

The transmission route of otitic meningitis has been roughly described above. Its pathogens should also be deeply understood. According to the opinions of general scholars, although staphylococcus, diplococcus, etc., can all cause this disease, hemolytic streptococcus is the most common.

The clinical symptoms and course of otitic meningitis often vary and differ from those of general meningitis. Generally speaking, it starts with an ear disease, followed by a disease of the intracranial meninges. To put it more plainly, the ear disease is its primary disease, and the meningeal disease is its secondary disease. It does not have the prodromal symptoms of epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis, such as chills, fever, vomiting, fatigue, headache, and sacral pain. However, if it is caused by acute otitis media, it can be the same as epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis, even with insomnia, restlessness, severe hearing impairment, and constant nausea. The common symptom of general otitis media is that the higher the body temperature, the more severe the clouding of consciousness, nuchal rigidity, hyperactive tendon reflexes, and gradually Kernig's sign also appears. The feet twitch, and the pupils also change, just like general epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis. Often, those caused by streptococcus do not have severe prodromal symptoms; there may be no digestive symptoms such as nausea and vomiting, only systemic discomfort like a cold, a slight increase in body temperature, and only mild headache, or even no headache. The clinical symptoms do not seem like meningitis, but once it changes, many severe symptoms suddenly appear and slowly transition to a state of paralysis. At this time, even with all kinds of treatments, there is little effect, and only death ensues.

The course of general otitic meningitis is generally several days to a week. If it is related to hemolytic streptococcus, death is inevitable within three days, even within twenty-four hours. It is extremely dangerous if it is not discovered and treated early.

In short, otitic meningitis, like epidemic cerebrospinal meningitis, is a very dangerous infectious disease. Although it is not often seen clinically, one must not underestimate ear diseases as minor illnesses and fail to treat them. If it unfortunately spreads to meningitis, it will be too late for regret!

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued) 226

— Zhou Mengbai

8. _Perilla frutescens_, Breit. Var. _Typica_ Makino

(Plant) Originally produced in China, it can be cultivated everywhere. It is an annual herb. The stem is square, the whole plant is covered with short hairs, the opposite leaves have long petioles and dentate green, sharp pointed tips. Terminal or axillary one-sided spicate inflorescences appear in summer and autumn, opening white small labiate flowers. The achene is slightly spherical.

(Component) The seeds contain approximately 40% fatty oil (perilla oil). The main components of this oil are glycerides of unsaturated fatty acids such as Olensaure and Linolensaure, mixed with a small amount of Palmitin. The iodine value of perilla oil is around 200, which is one of the highest iodine values among known vegetable oils.

(Uses) The seeds can be used to make perilla oil. Perilla oil has extremely strong drying properties and can be used to manufacture oil paper, umbrellas, etc.

9. _Perilla frutescens_, Breit. var. _Crispa_, Decne

(Plant) Originally produced in China, it can be cultivated everywhere. It is an annual herb. The whole plant is very similar to _Perilla frutescens_, except that the leaves are purple and the flowers are light purple. The whole plant has a distinctive aroma.

Green _Perilla frutescens_ is a good variety of _Perilla frutescens_. The leaves are green, and the flowers are white.

(Crude drug) _Perilla_ Seed (Semen _Perillae_) is collected from its seeds. This product is yellowish-brown or dark-brown particles, approximately 1.5 mm in diameter. The weight of 100 particles is approximately 0.2 grams. The odor has a distinctive aroma.

_Perilla_ Leaf (Folium _Perillae_) is collected from its leaves and dried. This product is broadly ovate, approximately 10.6 cm long, with sharp tips and serrated edges. The leaf surface has obvious wrinkles and is purple in color. The petiole is approximately 1 cm long. The odor has a distinctive aroma.

(Component) The whole plant contains approximately 0.5% essential oil. The main component is Perillaaldehyde Croh140 (55%). This substance has the characteristic aroma of this plant, and its structural formula is as follows.

(Medicinal use) Traditionally, _Perilla_ leaves and _Perilla_ seeds have been used as aromatic stomachic medicines, and also as expectorant and diuretic medicines.

(Other uses) _Perilla_ oil is used as a flavoring for pastries. According to Japanese scholar Mr. Furukawa, _Perilla_ oil has extremely strong preservative power. For example, 20 cm of _Perilla_ oil can completely preserve one stone of soy sauce. Also, something has a sweetness equivalent to 2000 times that of sugar and also has preservative power.

10. _Pelctranthus rugosus_, Makino

(Plant) Grows wild in the mountains and fields, it is a perennial herb. The stem reaches 1-1.5 meters in height, and the whole plant is densely covered with short hairs. The leaves are opposite, petiolate, ovate, with dentate edges and sharp tips. Terminal cymose inflorescences appear in autumn, opening light purple labiate flowers. The achenes are small.

(Component) The whole plant contains Plectranthin, a crystalline bitter substance. This substance has an extremely strong bitter taste, and the bitter taste is not obvious until it is in a 400,000-fold aqueous solution. Administering 0.4 grams of this substance internally to a dog, or injecting 0.1 grams subcutaneously into a dog, does not cause any symptoms. Therefore, this substance is used as a harmless bitter medicine.

(Medicinal use) In Japanese folk medicine, it is used as a bitter stomachic medicine, and it is also commonly used for abdominal pain. The plant name _Enmeiso_ (延命草) means "life-prolonging herb." _Wakan Sansai Zue_ (和漢三才圖會) says: "It is said that a traveler was dying of abdominal pain in the mountains. Kōbō-Daishi (弘法大師) climbed the mountain and encountered him, and had him eat this herb, and he immediately recovered. Afterwards, all tests proved effective, so it was named _Teimeiso_ (定命草)."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Pessimistic View on Negotiations with Japan 227

— Wo

The tense situation and the feeling of an impending storm seemed to dissipate after Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe's meeting with President Chiang. The situation suddenly eased, creating the impression of turning hostility into friendship. This is generally how the public perceives it. However, after carefully considering the Sino-Japanese problem, I remain pessimistic about the negotiations with Japan.

Japan's rhetoric in its negotiations with China invariably revolves around "friendship" and "sincerity." Friendship and sincerity are certainly welcome, but they are often abstract terms. The Sino-Japanese negotiations are, in reality, about conflicting interests, where friendship and sincerity have little place. If negotiations on an issue lead to a breakdown and resort to force, naturally, peace-loving countries like ours would not want this outcome. Even our aggressive neighbor, fond of war, would likely avoid it, as resorting to force would inevitably lead to significant sacrifices for both sides, regardless of who emerges victorious. Therefore, the talk of friendship and sincerity is merely diplomatic hypocrisy, devoid of genuine meaning.

Even in terms of friendship and sincerity, there are limits to friendship and inherent qualities to sincerity. Suppose Party A makes a demand on Party B, and Party B fulfills it to their satisfaction. In that case, Party A would naturally be pleased, considering it genuine friendship and sincere cooperation. However, can Party B be satisfied, friendly, or sincere? If Party B cannot meet the demands, they will inevitably accuse the other side of lacking sincerity and friendship. Therefore, sincerity and friendship are entirely dependent on the issue of mutual rights and cannot be resolved by empty words.

In the current diplomatic situation, although the tense atmosphere between the two sides has eased somewhat after Sangjima's visit to China and Kawagoe's meeting with Chiang, the Japanese side still insists on the special status of North China and joint anti-communist defense. This stance is vastly different from our principle of mutual benefit and equality and the preservation of territorial sovereignty. If the Japanese side adheres to this policy and refuses to back down, the hope for peace is minimal. Therefore, the outcome of peace or tension depends entirely on whether the Japanese authorities can thoroughly understand the situation. The key lies with the Japanese side, not with our country.

Furthermore, according to a report from the China United Press in Tokyo, Japan is determined to obtain North China, intending to adopt a "take the substance, avoid the name" approach. The so-called "take the substance, avoid the name" means occupying North China in reality without the official title, implementing economic aggression in lieu of territorial occupation. Japan has employed numerous approaches in its negotiations with our country, but they all boil down to the same thing: a hundred changes that do not deviate from their core purpose. This is, in fact, a major misjudgment in the policy of the Japanese authorities. The Japanese side constantly proclaims the principle of co-existence and co-prosperity. China and Japan are not only geographically connected but also share common interests. They are not only of the same culture but also interdependent like lips and teeth. Today, while Japan advocates this principle, they fail to fully understand it, seeking only their own immediate interests and neglecting long-term goals. Truly, their policymakers are irresponsible.

Therefore, if the Japanese side truly wishes to establish friendly and sincere cooperation with us, it must first abandon its aggressive ambitions, remove its menacing facade, and engage in open and honest discussions on mutual interests. This would not only benefit China and Japan but also the future of East Asia. If the Japanese side fails to consider this, the consequences will be beyond our imagination.

Wilderness Crossing 228

— Si

— No one on the wild ferry, the boat floats adrift.

When such a poetic scene appeared before my eyes, I was admiring it silently, wearing tattered clothes and carrying the heart of a wanderer.

It was the early autumn season. In the south, a cool breeze began to blow, and a unique, nameless fragrance drifted into my nostrils, gradually intoxicating me within the embrace of nature, placing me within a most beautiful landscape painting, where I began to dream the rosy dreams of youth.

However, I was wandering! And I was threatened by hunger! The cold days were fast approaching! Where was I to go?

I crossed my legs and sat on the grass. In front of me was a quiet stream, the water as clear as a mirror, only rippling slightly when the wind brushed across its surface. The stream was not wide, but I looked around and saw no bridge. The only way to cross the bank was by ferry. So, I gazed across to the other side, where the fields were green tinged with yellow, presenting the sight of half-ripened crops and sparse houses. Seen from afar, the houses looked even smaller, like accessories in a watercolor painting. The trees were indistinguishable, and further away, the snakelike mountains meandered, stubbornly crouching on the land. The sky was vast, an expanse of blue, with the white clouds characteristic of autumn flying and darting about. The sun shone brightly, illuminating everything with clarity and tranquility. It was truly a captivating scene.

Gazing at the distant fields, quietly... the wind whispered in my ears... the sun smiled happily! I felt an indescribable emotion, and I calmed down for a while.

Finally, I discovered the unmanned wild ferry lying on the stream to the left, with a support pole standing there. It floated on the surface of the water, with one side leaning against the grass. Upon discovering this wild ferry, I got up from the grass and ran over to it.

I should go to the other side, where there were houses and smoke rising, weren't there?

But I stopped beside the wild ferry, hesitating. This watercolor-like scene; here beside the stream in autumn, could I not quietly enjoy the happiness that nature had bestowed? I stood there woodenly, my heart pounding! It would ruin the scenery to load myself onto this wild ferry and cross to the other side! But I was so hungry! I was plunged into great anxiety.

The sound of light footsteps approaching from behind in the grass startled me from my thoughts. Appearing beside me was a hunched old man, holding a pipe but not smoking it. He sized me up and then began to speak:

"You're standing here by the stream, staring at the water. What are you thinking? You're new here, aren't you? Where are you planning to go?"

"I was wondering if this wild ferry could carry me to the other side," I replied, facing his wrinkled face. "If I have to walk, where is the bridge? Can you tell me?"

"There is a bridge, but you have to walk five more li to the east. But it's almost lunchtime now."

He turned his face away, and I turned my face away as well. In the near distance, across a short field, the chimney of a farmhouse was smoking. At the same time, I saw a girl in blue cloth walking towards us, smiling and revealing two rows of white teeth, with one hand placed on her forehead to shield her eyes from the sunlight. The old man knew that his daughter had come to call him to lunch, and he invited me to go back with him. I declined... until the charming farm girl insisted that I stay here until the afternoon before leaving, I submitted.

What a bountiful lunch it was—I marveled in my heart. Leaving the farmhouse, I was accompanied by the old man's daughter, who said she would take me to the bridge. I refused, thanking her sincerely... Before we knew it, we had returned to the wild ferry, where there was still a cool autumn breeze, a bright field, and rippling water.

"Let's part here," I said, my voice trembling.

She initially kept her head down; after hearing my words, she raised it and, facing the distant fields, said to me:

"By this gurgling stream, I have seen off countless travelers. They have all gone and never returned. Where are you going? Are you just going to flow like this stream, flowing, flowing, all the way ahead?"

"I am a wanderer..." I said.

We parted silently! I went east to the bridge to cross to the other side, leaving the wild ferry and the farm girl behind, moving forward on my own, without looking back.

The Mule Train 229

— Jin Ge

It's October!

The camellias, two zhang tall, are bursting with bright red flowers. The sight is so dense that from afar, it looks like a piece of red cloth has been dropped in mid-air. The sun struggles to penetrate the thick layers of flowers, its light strangely weak, as if filtered through a dense, thick red gauze, with a hint of ethereal red.

The mountain sparrows constantly flutter among the camellia trees, incessantly pecking at the branches with their hard beaks.

A gust of mountain wind blows, scattering the bright red petals into the sky, dancing for a long while before slowly drifting down, densely, like a rain of red. The ground resembles a newly laid red carpet, soft and fluffy, and even fragrant.

It is extremely quiet in this mountain, almost to the point where you can hear the footsteps of ants. Except for the occasional mule train passing through, (Note 1) it's rare for anyone to pass by here. So, the mountain is shrouded in loneliness all day long.

A dark mass, estimated to be around five hundred mules. The copper bell on the lead mule rings "ding-dong" with the mountain wind. The hooves beat out a dull rhythm, and on the back of each mule is a wooden pack saddle laden with goods. Following behind, spaced by dozens of mules, is a young man in a sheepskin vest, adorned with silver coins as buttons, wearing straw sandals with red laces. His trousers are pulled up high, and his face is a ruddy color, with strong arms and legs. He holds a leather whip in his hand, gently flicking it at the few lagging animals.

"Old Li, why don't we 'kai shao' yet?" (Note 2) says a man with a face full of sweat. He spits and wipes his sweat with his right sleeve.

"Who knows? It's boring to travel like this," says the man called Old Li.

"You lecher! There are no women here, of course you're bored!"

Ha... ha... The two laughed.

Brothers,

Keep at it!

Keep moving on,

Find an inn at the market town tonight!

The inn has a pretty girl,

The leader, riding a horse, catches up from behind, singing as he passes the brothers. Then, the brothers instinctively join in the song!

With a beautiful face,

And gleaming black hair,

Her delicate hands serve tea,

They sing loudly, the song echoing in the mountain valley, strangely pleasant. The brothers' feet gain strength, and the dying troop is once again filled with vigorous energy.

The night gradually descends, the earth draped in a layer of black gauze. The mountain wind howls, frighteningly. It is two days before the first quarter moon, so the moon is just a sliver, its light faint, with only a few scattered stars. The clouds are racing quickly. If it were not for the faint moonlight, the mountain would be completely plunged into darkness.

"Kai shao!" the leader calls out, raising his left arm.

"Brothers in the back, hurry up and catch up!"

"Hurry up, it's time for dinner!"

... A chaotic, joyful tone.

Sure enough, the brothers in the back surge forward like a tide. The leader orders the removal of the pack saddles and dispatches some brothers to graze the animals, while others go to find large stones and firewood. Only about ten remain to guard the pack saddles.

They skillfully select three stones of roughly the same size and arrange them in a triangle. They place the pot on top and start a fire underneath to cook the meal.

"Brothers, you've worked hard today, eat up! Have a hearty meal!" the leader says kindly.

"Let's all eat our fill!" A cheer erupts from their hearts.

After the meal, those who went to find firewood return with it, the mules are all tethered, and the remaining brothers, with nothing to do, smoke and chat. (To be continued)

Ballad Singing 231

Cao Xiaoying's "Yu Qing Ting" (Jade Dragonfly)

Zhongxi (1040), 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM. Opening: One of the Twenty-Four Filial Exemplars, "Zeng Shen Bites His Finger in Heartfelt Pain"

In a remote and desolate little village,

Farmers, woodcutters, scholars, and fishermen fill the town.

Recluses often emerge from the deep mountains,

Passing their days behind brushwood gates and thatched doors.

Most are leisurely and refined guests,

Secretly lamenting and writing poetry under the moon.

There was a handsome young woodcutter,

Who turned out to be the virtuous Zeng Shen, carrying firewood into the mountains.

He was a disciple of Confucius, receiving his teachings,

Caring for his mother with utmost filial piety.

Everyone in the village knew of the filial son Zeng,

And the whole town spread the word of his goodness.

One day, Zeng Shen went into the mountains carrying an axe,

To chop wood and buy rice for his dear mother.

Unexpectedly, a guest arrived at his home,

Leaving Zeng's mother at a loss as to how to entertain the visitor.

Her purse was empty, with no good solution,

Having neither wine nor food nor money.

She waited anxiously for her son's quick return, but he was nowhere to be seen.

Knowing their close maternal bond,

With a breath connecting them, they responded to each other.

Biting her finger with a resolute heart,

Zeng Shen felt an unbearable pain in his heart.

He hurriedly returned home with firewood,

And knelt down to ask his mother the reason.

Zeng's mother immediately opened her mouth and said,

"A guest has just arrived at our humble abode.

Because you haven't returned and I have few means,

I bit my finger to send you a message, ordering you home."

What a truly filial son, the sage Zeng Shen,

Such profound affection is rare in the world.

The fine hairs on the animal, separate from the fur, know the ruler.

Nüwa refined stones to mend the sky's flaw.

She left behind a dull and useless stone.

Having endured countless years of wind, frost, heat, and cold,

At the foot of Great Waste Mountain, it shone.

The Boundless Monk guided him with words.

The Vague Immortal brought him home.

The stone gained sentience and entered a mother's womb.

Born into the Jia family, with noble lineage.

The milk name Baoyu was not unintentional.

For at birth, he came into the world with jade in his mouth.

Lady Dowager Shi cherished him like a treasure,

Often worrying about wind and rain harming him.

His every move was attended by maids.

Then came the beautiful Lin Daiyu,

Ranking her first among the Twelve Beauties.

From childhood, they had a special connection,

Whispering intimately and staying by each other's side.

Applying rouge and powder near delicate eyebrows.

What a romantic and unrestrained young master Jia.

But at the mention of diligent study, he frowned.

To repay his parents' toil, he reluctantly went to the autumn examinations.

Water flows east and never returns.

The scattered cups and plates are not arranged as one wishes.

Meeting in the Bamboo Forest

The brother drags her into the bamboo forest.

Ah. The two of them play until the sun sets.

The mother scolds her daughter as a wicked spirit.

Why did you take so long to fetch water this morning?

Why is your hair disheveled?

Where did the yellow mud on your back come from?

The daughter tells her mother the road was difficult.

Why did it take so long to fetch water this morning?

The wind blew my hair into disarray.

The yellow mud on my back is from the embankment.

Movies

Streamlined Comedy of 1936, "Little Lingzi" to be Released Soon 234

The new Star Motion Picture Production "Little Lingzi," following "Night of Revelry" at the Jincheng Theater, is a good movie that is very much worth recommending. This film has been completed for a long time, but has only been released recently due to the congestion of new films from various companies in the theaters.

"Little Lingzi" tells the story of a village girl who is tempted by vanity and profit and runs into the city as the central theme. The author here strongly exposes the sins of the metropolis. This current society, which creates all sins, devours a pure and innocent little girl. This is a work with very high social value, and it is worthy of our attention.

Zhao Dan and Shu Xiuwen in "Qingming Season" 235

This play is praised as a streamlined comedy of 1933. The whole play has a bright and harmonious tone. Those who have seen the preview have praised it as having the style of an American film.

The director is Mr. Cheng Bugao, and he has put a lot of effort into the handling of this play. The leading actors are Tan Ying, Zhao Dan, Mei Xi, Gong Jianong, etc.

Tan Ying has achieved extraordinary results here, and her role is also the most important one. She has made extraordinary efforts here, and will undoubtedly gain a new evaluation. Zhao Dan and Mei Xi, one playing a young master of the city and the other playing a farmer in the countryside, both have excellent performances.

Amateur Actors and "The Forties" Co-star in "Sai Jinhua" 236

Amateurs have given way to avoid head-to-head competition, hoping they can join hands

We heard months ago that amateur actors were preparing to perform "Sai Jinhua," but the search for a suitable female lead delayed the performance until a graduate of the Art Academy, named Xu Wuyin, was introduced to play the role of Sai Jinhua. However, while the amateur actors were asking Ouyang Yuqian to direct the play, "The Forties" also announced that they would perform the play and had signed a contract with Jincheng to perform it at the end of the month.

At the same time, "The Forties" also wanted to invite Ouyang Yuqian to direct, and Ouyang Yuqian contacted both parties about this matter, hoping that they could cooperate, because a head-to-head competition would cause losses to both sides in terms of time, energy, and money, and besides, they should be joining hands.

But there was no result. So the amateur actors held a general discussion on how to deal with this matter. After discussion, it was decided that "Sai Jinhua" must be performed, because there was no suitable script to perform at the moment, and to avoid a head-to-head competition, the amateur actors wrote a letter to "The Forties" in a spirit of friendship, asking them to perform at the end of the month, while the amateurs would postpone it to the end of next month or the beginning of December, performing for a week at the Carlton. However, for the sake of the actors' energy, it would be divided into two stages, with "China Travel Service" taking over in between.

This method is very good, but it is hoped that the two troupes will join hands immediately after performing "Sai Jinhua," and we wish them success!

Valuable Harvest of Newsreel 237

Close-up Taken When Hu Hanmin Was in the Coffin, to Be Released at the Same Time as "Mother's Love"

When Mr. Hu Hanmin's remains were in the coffin, Minxin sent photographer Luo Jinghao to Guangzhou to shoot a newsreel. At that time, there were dozens of film companies competing to shoot the news, but none of them were allowed, except for Minxin, which was specially allowed to photograph all the details of the coffin. Afterwards, other companies planned to jointly invest in the purchase of the newsreel, but Minxin decided to keep it and did not sell it. It is said that this valuable newsreel and other Minxin newsreels will be released at the same time as the first production of "Mother's Love."
